Current Commentary

Aviation to Save the Nation - Sui 21

Speaking of saving the nation, there are indeed countless threads to untangle at the moment. It is difficult to know where to begin. However, making efforts to develop aviation can at least be considered the most practical aspect of the work of saving the nation. Modern warfare has already shifted from a flat plane to a three-dimensional one. This means that the key to determining victory in modern warfare is no longer on land or at sea, but in the air. The destructive power of aircraft is greater than that of any other combat weapon. It can turn a city into ruins in an instant and render the power of any army or navy useless. It can even determine the final victory or defeat in an instant. We only need to recall the devastation and terror inflicted upon us by the Japanese army's bombers and fighter planes during the January 28th Shanghai Incident to know that what is being said here is not an exaggeration. Not only was this the case during the January 28th Incident, but the injuries suffered by the Northeast Volunteer Army were due more to bombing from aircraft than to pressure from Japanese heavy artillery, tanks, and other powerful weapons. Therefore, at present, we can simply assert, "Without aviation, there is no national defense."

However, Japanese aircraft are still the most immature among the current great powers. It was only in the 20th year of the Meiji era that Chuhachi Ninomiya began to study aircraft in Japan. It was not until December of the 23rd year of the Meiji era that the first aircraft model was made, which could only fly a short distance over five rooms. It was not until the beginning of the Taisho era that there were relatively modern aircraft exercises. By the time the European War began, various European countries had already adopted aircraft as the main combat weapon, while Japan had only four, which surprisingly played a decorative role when fighting the Germans in our Qingdao. Who knew that in these ten years, they had exerted all their efforts to promote it throughout the country, and finally established the air force strength that cannot be easily underestimated today. This is of course because they fundamentally recognized the great value of the air force in national defense.

Now let us examine our aviation strength. It is enough to make one's heart chill and one's courage fail. Alas, on such a vast land, not to mention offensive aviation, but even defensive aviation is completely unequipped. Not only is this the case in the provinces and regions, but even the air defense of the capital is in fact no different. If the statement "Without aviation, there is no national defense" is indeed true, can we still speak of national defense? Can our future still be imagined? Although the former three northeastern provinces did have several aircraft, during the September 18th Incident in Shenyang, they were all seized by the enemy without any resistance.

Even now, the Japanese are still tirelessly working on the construction of aviation. They have built many underground shelters and installed anti-aircraft guns and sound detectors in Tokyo, Osaka, Nagoya, and other places. They have conducted two large-scale air defense drills within the past year. Even among the civilians, there is the same kind of frenzy. Many army and navy personnel voluntarily donate patriotic and nation-serving aircraft. Other national organizations or individuals are even more eager to offer domestically produced aircraft to be incorporated into the air force. As of June 19, 1932, young students had saved their candy money to purchase military aircraft, such as the "Middle School Student" and "Elementary School Student" aircraft. Other patriotic aircraft donated by civilians have reached more than 40. For the sake of aggression, they are still working so hard on aviation. For the sake of self-defense, shouldn't we rise up and catch up urgently?

This time, various circles in Shanghai are holding Aviation to Save the Nation Propaganda Week starting yesterday, planning to make efforts to publicize it during this week so that the people have a deep understanding of the value of aviation. We believe that this kind of work is of great significance. Indeed, "Without aviation, there is no national defense." And only the air force can deal with the enemy's air force when it devastates a certain city. Therefore, we believe that building aviation and developing aviation is the most urgent task for our country at present. We hope that in the shortest possible time, every county in the country will have at least one aircraft.

However, we further hope that in the future, all troops and ordnance will belong to the "nation" and not be "privately owned," because "private ownership" is not enough to benefit the country, but rather enough to bring disaster to the country. Our hope for the development of aviation is also the same.

The So-Called Modern Japanese Diplomacy Obeys the Nods of Military Cliques 22

Member of the Seiyukai Party Questioned in the House of Representatives Yesterday

(Tokyo) The spokesman for the Seiyukai Party, Ashida, questioned the diplomatic incidents with a very sharp tone in the House of Representatives this afternoon, demanding that the Foreign Minister and the Army Minister give a clear answer as to whether Japan has a definite diplomatic policy and whether the Ministry of Foreign Affairs only follows the instructions of the Army. He said that Japan is currently being dragged blindly to a dangerous and dark precipice, with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs being nothing more than a rubber stamp for the Ministry of the Army. Important positions in Manchuria are monopolized by the Army. Although the existence of the current cabinet is mainly for the purpose of unifying Japan's policy towards Manchuria, the general impression is that the responsibility for guiding Manchuria is now solely borne by the Army. Ashida also criticized the government with the following points: 1) Japan's unnecessarily harsh attitude in Geneva and its disputes over trivial matters; 2) Japan lacks a fundamental policy towards the League of Nations and Manchuria; 3) Although Foreign Minister Uchida has stated the importance of friendship and cooperation between China, Japan, and Manchuria, Japan has not yet taken concrete steps to establish friendship and cooperation between China, Japan, and Manchuria. Ashida also spoke freely about the necessity of improving Japan's relations with the United States and Russia, saying that there is a situation that makes people deeply believe that Japan's diplomatic policy is controlled by the Army, which is a shameful thing. Foreign Minister Uchida replied that there is no reason to worry about the situation between Japan, Russia, and the United States. Japan's foreign policy has always cooperated with the military authorities, but it has never handled foreign affairs according to the instructions of the Army. Army Minister Araki also replied that the military authorities are working with all parties to resolve the Manchurian problem and that the Army authorities have never acted independently in this incident. (Reuters, 23rd)

Expansion of Armaments, the London Treaty is Equal to Waste Paper 23

(Tokyo) The plenary session of the House of Representatives opened at 1:00 PM today. Uchida Shinya (Seiyukai) immediately took the podium and said that the military expenditure in this budget proposal reached a huge amount of 800 million yen, which exposed the unreasonableness and deception at the time of the conclusion of the London Treaty (his words refer to the Minseito Party). Is this naval replenishment plan limited to one year, or will there be a second replenishment? When will the future expenses required for the Manchurian Incident be submitted? How does the current government view the decision of troop strength, which Prime Minister Hamaguchi once answered was in the hands of the government? Furthermore, he said that recently there has been an atmosphere in the military that denies party politics and capitalism, and what is the truth about this? After descending from the podium, Navy Minister Osumi immediately replied that this replenishment plan is one part of the second replenishment plan, but there is no atmosphere within the Navy that denies the party. (Editor's note: Hualianshe reported that Navy Minister Osumi answered Uchida's question in the Lower House today, saying that the Navy Province has a second naval replenishment plan, with total expenses of approximately 460 million yen, which will be a continuing project for three or four years to complete this plan. Since the London Treaty, this case has been questioned in the Diet every time, but no responsible person has given a clear answer. Osumi explicitly stated without hesitation that the current confrontation between Japan and the United States is an undeniable fact, and the detailed content will be announced at the budget general meeting.) After Prime Minister Saito and Nagai, Minister of Colonial Affairs, answered questions on the issue of supreme command, Army Minister Araki replied that the idea of denying the party is because of the individual differences, so the military department cannot answer this kind of question itself.

Army Minister Araki Leads a Minority Military to Carry Out Aggression 24

Next, Ashida Hitoshi (Seiyukai) took the podium to ask questions: 1. Isn't Army Minister Araki leading a minority military to handle Manchuria? Why doesn't the whole country unanimously handle the Manchurian problem? 2. What is the policy after applying Article 15, Paragraph 4 of the League of Nations Covenant? 3. What are the countermeasures against the United States and Russia? Foreign Minister Uchida answered that it is unexpected that there is no national policy on Manchuria, and the Japan-Manchuria defense alliance according to the protocol is this policy. The military department is said to be entirely in charge of Manchuria, but at the time of the incident, the nature of the incident made it impossible to determine the political aspects of "Manchukuo". Regardless of civil or military officials, the involvement of Japanese in "Manchukuo" will gradually decrease as "Manchukuo" develops.

Before the League of Nations Assembly, It is Said that There is a Reconciliation Method 25

As for the policy towards the League of Nations, there may be a method of reconciliation before the General Assembly on February 1, so it cannot be said whether to withdraw or not. For this reason, future diplomatic relations with China are a difficult problem. If the Chinese are aware and start direct negotiations, it will be easy to solve. In addition, both the United States and Russia have gradually become understanding of Japan. Army Minister Araki also replied that there is no such idea as a soldier carrying the "Manchukuo", and it is necessary for the whole country to be united. The fact that today's military department and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are working together is something that has not happened in 30 years. After the Foreign Minister and the Army Minister answered, Kiyose Ichiro (Kokumin Domei) questioned the necessity of renewing the administrative organization and implementing a standing committee in the parliament. Prime Minister Saito replied that the establishment of a standing committee needs to be carefully considered. After Finance Minister Takahashi answered questions about the renewal of the administrative organization, Foreign Minister Uchida said that the border issue between Japan, Manchukuo, and Russia has also been proposed by the other party and is currently under negotiation. There were also answers from Minister of Education Hatoyama and Minister of Justice Oyama.

What Concessions are Ultimately Necessary in the Policy Towards China? 26

Later, Matsumoto Shio (Minseito) questioned diplomatic issues. Prime Minister Saito answered that he hoped for a perfect countermeasure for the League of Nations. Foreign Minister Uchida answered that the countermeasures for Manchuria are fixed and will not change, while the countermeasures for China will be carried out in the spirit of coordination, so he is preparing for the necessary concessions, and his sincerity is well known to the Chinese side. (Dentsu, 23rd)

Duan Qirui Departs from Nanjing for Shanghai 27

Chiang Kai-shek Personally Sees Him Off

Yesterday Accompanied Chiang to Pay Respects at Sun Yat-sen's Mausoleum

(Nanjing) Duan Qirui rose early on the 23rd, having breakfast at 8:00 AM. The Lixingshe (Society for Encouragement of Morality) prepared exquisite vegetarian food for him in advance. He Yingqin, Zhu Peide, and others hosted a farewell luncheon for Duan at Lixingshe. In the evening, fellow Anhui natives Zhang Zhizhong, Wu Zhongxin, Zhang Wohua, Xu Shiying, and others held a public banquet for Duan at Lixingshe. In the morning, Zhang Qun, Song Ziwen, and others visited, engaging in lengthy talks. In the afternoon, Dai Jitao, Ju Zheng, and others paid visits. At 2:30 PM, Chiang Kai-shek arrived at the society and accompanied Duan to pay respects at the mausoleum. Upon descending the steps, Chiang invited Duan to tour Tangshan, but Duan politely declined. At 4:00 PM, they returned to Lixingshe. Chiang extended an audience to Wu Guangxin, Duan Honggang, Wei Zonghan, and others. Chiang departed at 5:30 PM, and Duan then went to visit Chairman Lin Sen. Lin reciprocated the visit at 6:00 PM. It was decided that they would take a train to Shanghai in the evening. Chiang dispatched Zhang Qun to see them off and instructed the railway bureau to prepare four first-class carriages and one chartered carriage for Duan's use. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) Duan Qirui retired to bed after attending Chiang's banquet on the evening of the 22nd. On the morning of the 23rd, he rose at 6:30 AM and took a walk, returning to his room at 7:00 AM to recite scriptures. He had breakfast at 8:00 AM. Duan favored vegetarian food. After breakfast, he met with Central Committee member Zhang Qun and a dozen or so disciples serving in military organs. At 11:00 AM, Song Ziwen paid a visit. At noon, He Yingqin and other high-ranking military officers hosted a farewell banquet, with a lively atmosphere. Duan was very pleased. At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, Chiang planned to accompany Duan to pay respects at the mausoleum. If there were no delays in the evening, Central Committee member Zhang Qun would accompany him to Shanghai. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) On the 23rd, various important figures visited Duan at Lixingshe. At 11:00 AM, Song Ziwen visited for 20 minutes. At 11:30 AM, Chairman Lin Sen visited for 15 minutes. At 11:45 AM, Luo Wengan visited for 15 minutes. At 2:00 PM in the afternoon, Dai Jitao and Ju Zheng visited for half an hour. At 2:30 PM in the afternoon, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek accompanied him to pay respects at the mausoleum. At 4:35 PM, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek conferred with Mr. Duan again until departing at 5:20 PM. Other visitors included Zhu Peide, He Yaozu, Wu Zhongxin, Pan Weiyue, Yang Yongtai, Zhang Foming, Yang Jie, Zhang Qun, Chen Yi, Lin Jing, Yang Huancai, Hu Ruoyu, Tang Shengzhi, the Panchen Lama, Li Guojie, Ma Xiaojun, Xiong Bin, Shi Ying, Wang Yongbin, Chen Guofu, Ma Xiang, Liang Hancao, Wang Zhao, Gao Lingxiao, Duan Ruoyu, Zhou Yawei, Di Luowa Hutuktu, Zhong Tiguo, Zhang Yisan, Ruan Yongqi, Zhang Peigang, and others, totaling over a hundred people. At noon, 34 military and political leaders, Shanghai notables, and others jointly hosted a banquet at Lixingshe to welcome Mr. Duan. In the evening at 6:00 PM, fellow Anhui natives Xu Shiying, Zhang Zhizhong, Wu Zhongxin, Zhang Wohua, and others also hosted a banquet at Lixingshe. Today, when paying respects at the mausoleum, Duan, Chiang, and Wu Guangxin rode in car number 318 to the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum. Those accompanying them included Wei Zonghan, Duan Yunkai, Dai Chuanxian, Xu Shiying, Ju Zheng, Zhang Qun, Peng Chunshi, Zhong Bojie, Zu Jingsheng, and more than a dozen others. Mr. Duan walked, but after reaching halfway, he was persuaded by everyone to switch to a rattan sedan chair to reach the memorial hall. Duan bowed once towards the portrait of Sun Yat-sen and presented a wreath. He then entered the memorial hall to view it, and upon exiting, he walked down, supported by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Although Mr. Duan is advanced in years, his spirit is still strong. After completing the mausoleum visit, he returned to Lixingshe to rest. After Chairman Chiang returned to Lixingshe, he immediately met with Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan, and Duan Yunkai. In the afternoon at 5:00 PM, Duan, accompanied by Xu Shiying, took a car to Chairman Lin Sen's private residence in Shibanqiao to return the visit. Other ministry heads were visited by Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan, and Duan Yunkai, who made return visits starting at 10:00 AM. Because Duan was traveling to Shanghai, the Ministry of Railways instructed the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Bureau to prepare a floral car and four sleeping cars for use. Duan himself originally planned to go to Shanghai tonight, but those around him, fearing that the night train would be too bumpy to sleep comfortably, requested that he depart this morning. Subsequently, Zhuang Yi from Shanghai was dispatched to Beijing to welcome him. Duan then decided to go to Shanghai at 11:45 PM that evening. Those accompanying him included Wu Guangxin, Wei Zonghan, Duan Yunkai, Xu Shiying, Zhang Qun, and others. After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Duan will rest for a few days and then travel to Hangzhou for sightseeing. He will likely stay in Shanghai for several months in the future. (Special dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) Duan Qirui's two-day stay in Nanjing was marked by a warm welcome from old acquaintances in Beijing. He departed for Shanghai on the evening of the 23rd, with a floral car attached to the night express. Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, dressed in plain clothes and with a small entourage, arrived at Lixingshe at 10:50 PM, spoke briefly, and then invited Duan and Wu Guangxin to board his own car, along with Zhang Qun, Xu Shiying, Zhang Wohua, Wei Zonghan, Duan Honggang, and others. They departed from the society. At 11:15 PM, they arrived at the station. Chu Minyi, He Yaozu, Yang Yongtai, Lu Chao, Zhang Zhizhong, and Chen Yi also arrived at the station to see them off. Duan wore a blue sable coat, cotton shoes with white soles, and appeared to be in better spirits than when he arrived in Beijing. Upon arriving at the station, Chiang personally helped Duan off the car. Duan walked briskly, nodding and smiling at the well-wishers. Chiang saw him into the carriage, spoke briefly, and then exited the station to return to his residence. The train departed at 11:45 PM. According to Xu Shiying, after arriving in Shanghai, Duan plans to reside at the World Cultural Association at 393 Fuxing Road. Once the weather warms, he plans to go to Hangzhou, retreat into the mountains, or travel to Putuo Mountain to study Buddhism. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

(Nanjing) Those who saw Duan Qirui off at the station on the evening of the 23rd included Wu Siyu, Chen Yi, Yu Feipeng, He Yaozu, Chu Minyi, Chiang Kai-shek, Lu Chao, and others. (Special dispatch, 23rd)

The Control Yuan Impeaches Chairman Gu Zhutong of Jiangsu Province 29

Regarding the Execution of Liu Yusheng, Manager of the Jiangsheng Newspaper

Illegally Detaining a Reporter and Refusing the Control Yuan's Investigation

(Nanjing) Control Yuan members Liu Eqing and Tian Jiongjin have impeached Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, regarding the execution of Liu Yusheng, manager of the Zhenjiang Jiangsheng Daily, by the Zhenjiang Garrison Headquarters, for illegally arresting and detaining him, and for resisting the investigation by the Control Yuan. The Control Yuan has assigned Control Yuan members Zhou Lisheng, Gao Yihan, and Li Menggeng to review the case, who have determined that he should be disciplined. In addition to notifying the Executive Yuan, the original case documents have been submitted to the National Government for review and implementation. The original impeachment document and the review report submitted to the National Government are recorded below:

Regarding the matter of impeaching Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, for illegally arresting and detaining Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily, and for resisting the investigation by the Control Yuan. The Provisional Constitution during the Period of Political Tutelage is the fundamental law during the period of political tutelage. All government officials and citizens should abide by it in order to promote constitutional government. According to Article 8 of Chapter 2 of said law, if a person is arrested or detained on suspicion of committing a crime, the agency executing the arrest or detention must, at the latest, transfer the person to the judicial organ for questioning within 24 hours. The person or others may also request a writ of habeas corpus within 24 hours in accordance with the law. Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, detained Liu Yusheng, manager of the Zhenjiang Jiangsheng Daily, at the Garrison Headquarters of the Provincial Security Department on July 26 of this year, and has not transferred him to the court for examination in accordance with the law for five months. This violates the Provisional Constitution and tramples on human rights, which is offense number one. According to Article 2 of the Organic Law of the Control Yuan, the Control Yuan may, in exercising its powers, inquire or investigate case files from various government offices and other public institutions. If there are any questions, the responsible personnel should be responsible for providing detailed answers. Furthermore, Article 1 of the Rules for the Use of Investigation Certificates clearly stipulates that investigators may use this certificate to go to various government offices and public institutions to investigate case files. The responsible personnel of the respective government offices or institutions must not refuse, and must not conceal the cases being investigated. According to the report of Ma Zhen, a staff member dispatched by this Yuan to investigate, when said staff member arrived at the provincial government to investigate the case, the Chairman not only failed to provide a full answer, but also resolutely refused to allow the review of the files, undermining the supervisory system and disregarding government orders, which is offense number two. Furthermore, the provincial government issued an order to the Provincial Public Security Bureau on July 20, stating that the Jiangsheng Daily violated Articles 19, Paragraphs 1 and 2 of the Publication Law regarding the stated corrections, and ordered the Director to immediately order the Jiangsheng Daily and its supplements to cease publication, and to secretly summon Liu Yusheng, the newspaper's manager, to the government for investigation. Article 23 of the Publication Law (see attachment to the investigation report) clearly stipulates that the power to prohibit publication or confiscate belongs to the Ministry of Interior. The Chairman illegally arrested and overstepped his authority, which is offense number three. Furthermore, the provincial government's letter to the provincial government stated that the Jiangsheng Daily supplement "Iron Rhinoceros" contained opinions that endangered public safety, and was handed over to the Garrison Headquarters for handling in accordance with Article 13, Paragraph 1 of the Provisional Regulations for Martial Law in the Jiangsu Provincial Capital (see attachment to the investigation report). The articles cited in the provincial government's secret document to the Public Security Bureau are different, which clearly indicates a different purpose and an intention to frame him, which is offense number four. Furthermore, the novels ("When") (Underling's Know-How) (Border Sound) (Dragon Boat Festival) published in the Jiangsheng Daily supplement "Iron Rhinoceros" only describe social life, and similar articles are published in various newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai from time to time. The Central Party Headquarters has not issued an order prohibiting publication, and the Ministry of Interior has no precedent of closing newspapers and arresting journalists for publishing such texts. The Chairman had no prior announcement prohibiting publication. It is already inappropriate to punish without teaching in an autocratic era, let alone today, which harms freedom of speech and undermines the spirit of the rule of law, which is offense number nine. Based on the above points, an impeachment should be filed immediately in accordance with the law. Please move to discipline Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and provide for immediate relief. Please notify the Executive Yuan and order the provincial government to swiftly transfer Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily, to the court for swift handling in accordance with the law, in order to maintain law and discipline and protect human rights. Is this appropriate? Respectfully submitted to the President for review. Control Yuan Members Liu Eqing and Tian Jiongjin. Also, the review report, regarding the matter of the review report. The case was assigned to the two Control Yuan members, Liu Eqing and Tian Jiongjin, to impeach Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, for illegally detaining Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily. After a joint review, it was unanimously agreed that the Chairman of the Provincial Government had violated the Provisional Constitution and the Publication Law, detained a journalist for five or six months, and disregarded the Organic Law of the Control Yuan and the Rules for the Use of Investigation Certificates by refusing to cooperate with the Yuan's investigators. This is an extreme case of illegal and abusive power. Therefore, Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, should be disciplined in accordance with the law. The Executive Yuan should be notified to order the Provincial Government to swiftly transfer Liu Yusheng to the court for interrogation in order to uphold human rights and promote the rule of law. Respectfully submitted to the President, Yu Youren. Control Yuan Members Zhou Lisheng, Gao Yihan, and Li Menggeng. Document submitted to the National Government, regarding the matter of submitting a request for disciplinary action. According to Control Yuan members Liu Eqing and Tian Jiongjin, Gu Zhutong, Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, illegally arrested and detained Liu Yusheng, manager of the Jiangsheng Daily, and resisted the investigation by the Yuan. A case for impeachment has been filed, which has been assigned to Control Yuan members Zhou Lisheng, Gao Yihan, and Li Menggeng for review. According to the report, it is believed that disciplinary action should be taken, and the Executive Yuan should be notified to order the Jiangsu Provincial Government to swiftly transfer Liu Yusheng to the court, etc. In accordance with this, in addition to notifying the Executive Yuan, a copy of the original case documents has been submitted to your esteemed government for review and implementation. Respectfully submitted to the National Government. (Special dispatch, 23rd)

Gu Mengyu Discusses the Organizational Law of the People's Political Council 35

Combining Regional and Occupational Elections

Since Chairman Chiang Kai-shek went to Hubei last year to supervise the suppression, the Red bandits in Hubei Province have been eliminated, and the Red bandits in Fujian Province have also been gradually wiped out by the 19th Route Army. Currently, only Jiangxi Province still has remaining bandits, stubbornly resisting, but after being surrounded by the National Army, they can be eradicated soon. In their declaration, the condition that the National Army would no longer advance on the Red bandits is self-explanatory. Recalling that after the September 18th Incident, Zhu Mao and others also issued a similar declaration, willing to unite against Japan, but during the January 28th Incident last year, when the National Army was transferred from Jiangxi to Shanghai to reinforce, the Red bandits followed closely, harassing our advance, causing the National Army's deployment to be delayed and the rescue to be unsuccessful, and the battle of Shanghai failed as a result. Thinking about it now, there is still regret. Now that the Red bandits are desperate, they are taking advantage of the Yuguan Incident to repeat their old tricks. If the Chinese people are not forgetful, they will not be deceived by their propaganda policies, causing the great cause of bandit suppression to fail and leaving behind a major problem for the future. There will be facts to prove it soon. (Central News Agency dispatch, 23rd)

A Passenger on a Beijing-Shanghai Train Robbed by Bandits 39

170 Silver Dollars Stolen

(Zhenjiang) At about 8:00 PM tonight, as the 26th Beijing-Xixiang section train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway passed the Gaozi Station, a bandit with a bayonet robbed a third-class passenger named Liu Junliang, stealing 170 silver dollars and a leather robe. Upon receiving the report, the police chief immediately supervised the entire team of police chiefs and officers, boarded a single locomotive, and set off at 8:50 PM to the scene of the incident to carry out the arrest. Unprecedented Great War in South America, Paraguayan and Bolivian Armies Battle Fiercely for Three Days, Hand-to-Hand Combat and Fierce Attacks Result in Over a Thousand Casualties 69

(Brazilian Capital) National News Agency, 22nd: The current fighting near the Nanawa fortress in the Chaco region can be regarded as the largest war in South American history. Although both Paraguayan and Bolivian capitals have successively issued contradictory war reports, the general public believes that the two countries have already entered into a major war to determine the future sovereignty of the Chaco Triangle. After three days of fierce fighting, with each side using wild artillery to bombard and engaging in physical charges, the Paraguayan Command claimed that Bolivian troops suffered more than 1,200 casualties and their morale was low. The Bolivian Command claimed that Bolivian troops were advancing steadily and that Paraguayan troops had suffered 1,000 casualties. At this time, both sides seem to have sufficient ammunition, which was transported to the front lines while the winter fighting slowed down. Bolivian operations are clearly being directed remotely by German General Kundt. In the last few hours, it has been heard that another 4,000 elite troops have been sent to the front lines, hoping to shift the situation. Both sides have strong air forces, reportedly commanded by several foreign officers. Although the battlefield is closer to the Paraguayan capital, there is no fear of air raids, as this war cannot last long due to transportation difficulties for both sides, difficulty in maintaining supplies, and continuous rain. February is the rainiest time of year, after which the roads will be muddy and transportation will become even more difficult, inevitably leading to a natural halt. However, both countries likely have no intention of accepting the proposal for an immediate ceasefire, withdrawal to original defenses, and waiting for mediation proposed by the neutral countries of the United States, Mexico, Cuba, Colombia, and Uruguay.

Intense Party Strife in Germany 70

Hitler's Followers March in Various Formations

Reuters dispatch, Berlin, 22nd: This afternoon's National Socialist Party rally was relatively peaceful, as there were thousands of police and three armored vehicles on scene to suppress any disturbances. Ten thousand National Socialist Party members braved the snow and cold to gather on Burgher Street, where they formed ranks and marched toward the cemetery nearby. Party leader Hitler held an unveiling ceremony at the cemetery for a memorial building dedicated to Wessel, a party member who was killed several years ago. Hitler said in his speech that the National Socialist Party will fight until Germany's disarray, suffering, and hunger are completely eradicated. The officiating priest quoted the words of Germany's greatest statesman, Bismarck, saying that even if the world is full of demons, Germans have nothing to fear, knowing only to fear God. There were many wreaths on the memorial building, and both the former German Emperor and the former Crown Prince sent wreaths. The unveiling ceremony passed peacefully without any incidents. However, before and after the meeting, there were several clashes between various parties. Communists piled bedding on top of garbage bins in the eastern end of Berlin and set them on fire to obstruct the National Socialist Party's march. The fire brigade was busy extinguishing the fires. According to a police report in the evening, a total of thirty-five people were injured and one hundred were arrested. In addition to using batons to disperse the crowd, police sometimes opened fire to repel the communists. Four police officers were stabbed with knives today, and several National Socialist Party members were attacked. The Communist Party stated that it will hold demonstrations for several days in a row this week to protest, and plans to convene a mass rally outside the old palace on January 24th after obtaining police permission.

Japanese House of Peers Discusses Communist Incident 71

Meeting Contents Strictly Secret

Communist and Police Engage in Fierce Battles

Dentsu dispatch, Tokyo, 23rd: The content of today's secret meeting of the House of Peers is reportedly related to the Communist Party incident. Justice Minister Oyama reported for forty minutes, after which questioning began. Matsumura Giichi of the Koseikai questioned whether it was necessary to investigate the source of funds used for the incident and to expose those behind them who provided support in order to fundamentally eliminate the ominous incident. Oyama replied that this matter is still under investigation and therefore cannot be reported.

Nichi-Rengo News Agency dispatch, Tokyo, 23rd: Most members of the Japanese Communist Party have reportedly been arrested by party authorities. However, the Special Higher Police Division of the Police Department has recently learned that remnants are still active and has also learned that a secret meeting was held in Hatagaya from the 15th. Police officers were dispatched to arrest them at the beginning of this month. After a fierce battle, five communist members were arrested. The whereabouts of Dr. Kawakami Hajime's daughter are still unknown, and the authorities are making every effort to search for her.

Reuters dispatch, Tokyo, 23rd: Seventeen Koreans have been arrested, reportedly for being members of the Communist Party and planning to organize a Communist Party in Korea.

Ninth Anniversary of Lenin's Death 72

TASS dispatch, Moscow, 22nd: Yesterday was the ninth anniversary of the death of Soviet revolutionary leader Lenin. Lenin passed away on January 21, 1924, in the village of Gorki near Moscow. A memorial meeting was held here yesterday at the largest Moscow Opera and Ballet Theatre. Party and government leaders and representatives from factories attended. Central Committee member Stanzki spoke about the socialist construction of the past nine years, pointing to the success of the Five-Year Plan in four years as proof of the gradual realization of Lenin's ideals. Stanzki also said that the Five-Year Plan was successful entirely due to Stalin's leadership, so when commemorating the heroes of the party, Stalin's contributions should not be forgotten.

TASS dispatch, Moscow, 23rd: All newspapers here have published articles on the ninth anniversary of Lenin's death, many of which are recollections of Lenin by old friends and comrades. "Pravda" declared in its editorial that the socialist construction of the Soviet Union is advancing in accordance with the path indicated by Lenin, and the success of the First Five-Year Plan is proof of this.

Greek Parliament Dissolved 73

National News Agency dispatch, Athens, 23rd: The Greek Parliament was dissolved by presidential decree this afternoon because it was about to pass a vote of no confidence in the government. However, at least one-third of the members protested fiercely. It is heard that general elections will be held in early March.

Havas dispatch, Athens, 22nd: The government has convened the Senate to meet tomorrow. Political figures believe that the government intends to dissolve the House of Representatives after convening the Senate, as Prime Minister Venizelos occupies a large majority in the Senate. Former Prime Minister Tsaldaris, leader of the People's Party, stated that if the government intends to dissolve the House of Representatives without first contacting it, the People's Party, which adheres to republicanism, will safeguard the republican system by various means.

Portuguese President Critically Ill 74

National News Agency dispatch, Lisbon, 23rd: Portuguese President General Carmona is currently suffering from pneumonia. As he is already sixty-three years old, there is cause for great concern.

British Famous Novelist Galsworthy Seriously Ill 75

Havas dispatch, Paris, 23rd: The New York Evening Post's European Continental Supplement reported that British literary giant Galsworthy, who won the Nobel Prize for Literature last year, suffered from anemia due to overwork last November and was unable to collect the award in person. Galsworthy is now seriously ill.

Far East Soviet Army 79

Tokyo Dispatch: According to the provisional estimate of Japan's trade with China for February released by the Japanese Ministry of Finance, as follows:

Compared to the Same Period Last Year:

Excess Exports: 4,988

Exports: 34,024, Increase of 22,789

Imports: 29,036, Increase of 8,964

Total: 63,060, Increase of 31,753

Namely, in November, Japan's trade with China (including the Liaodong Peninsula and Hong Kong) had exports of 34,024,000 yuan, imports of 29,036,000 yuan, and a total export and import value of 63,060,000 yuan, with an export surplus of 4,988,000 yuan after deducting the above. Compared with the same month last year, exports increased by 22,789,000 yuan (approximately 20%), and imports increased by 8,964,000 yuan (approximately 45%). Furthermore, calculating the full-year amount since January, exports amounted to 294,055,000 yuan (an increase of 14% compared to the previous year), and imports amounted to 206,442,000 yuan (a decrease of 12.7% compared to the previous year). The total full-year export surplus was 87,613,000 yuan, an increase of 65,928,000 yuan compared to the export surplus of 21,685,000 yuan in the previous year. Deployment of Northeast Reserve Soldiers 86

Incorporated into Four Brigades of Puppet Army

Will Head to the Front Soon

Changchun Dispatch: With the intense battles between Shanhaiguan and Jiukou continuing for days, some scattered information has been gleaned from those returning from within the关，but the actual situation remains difficult to ascertain. Recently, it has been possible to hear news from the Central Broadcasting Station through radio broadcasts, but even this cannot be relied upon, as the Japanese are using the Fanyang International Radio to broadcast confusing information in order to disrupt the sound waves, making it impossible to hear the messages from the Central Station. Rumors are rampant everywhere, prices are skyrocketing, and Japanese gold notes are depreciating daily. All show signs of unrest. However, the Japanese are making every effort to beautify the peace and are creating all kinds of information favorable to Japan for the League of Nations, while not mentioning a word about the battles of Shanhaiguan and Jiukou in order to block the sight and hearing of tens of millions of people, believing that this is a surefire strategy for controlling all of the Northeast. Major cities such as Jilin, Changchun, and Harbin, along with most merchants and workers' organizations, are secretly raising military funds, intending to remit them to Beiping and Tianjin for use as war funds. The Japanese are sending out detectives to search for this. The Shandong Fellow Countrymen's Association in Harbin has already been monitored by the Japanese military police. However, many individuals are remitting funds to Shanghai for transfer to Zhu Ziqiao for use as volunteer army funds. The puppet regime's traitors know that the situation is not good, but because Japanese surveillance has been very strict recently, gatherings of more than three people are not allowed. Therefore, most people dare not talk about the Shanhaiguan incident. Merchants and workers in various places, because the Central Government has made war preparations, believe that rescue is imminent. Many are winding down their businesses and returning to关, wanting to contribute to the military effort. However, the Japanese in Dalian, fearing that the puppet regime's secrets will be leaked to the outside world, have stopped outbound ship voyages, and banned Chinese people from returning to China. Therefore, those with ambitions can only return to their original places and await the national flag to be flown again.

The Nakamura Brigade of the 10th Japanese Division under Hirose Jujiro is scheduled to concentrate in Harbin within the next few days and head to 关 before the lunar new year. Four brigades are to be selected from the puppet army to go south, though this has been agreed in principle, the reorganization requires further study. The Japanese fear that if the puppet army reaches the front, they will not only mutiny, but kill the enemy in reverse, so they intend to select several thousand from among their reservists and incorporate them into the puppet army. Junior officers will also be Japanese, monitoring the puppet army as they depart. The reservists will be supplemented by those currently in the Northeast. The process of organization is underway. It is not yet decided which brigades of the puppet army will be sent.

While the Japanese army is exerting its utmost efforts to suppress all of the Northeast by force, Hanson, the US Consul General stationed in Harbin, has departed this month on the 16th on a mission of economic investigation. The Japanese government is paying close attention to the mission of the U.S. Consul (16th).

Suzhou

Anti-Japanese Association Punishes Treacherous Merchants 87

Wu Huangen, the owner of the Shenghe Coal Shop at Dashihui Bridge outside Xumen, specialized in selling enemy coal. In July of last year, the Anti-Japanese Association seized over 70 tons of enemy coal. At that time, due to the large quantity, it was inconvenient to transport it, so only coal samples were taken. Later, when they went to pick up the goods, the enemy coal had disappeared. In October, another 65 tons were seized, and the County Chamber of Commerce and the County Party Headquarters auctioned it off, obtaining 390 taels, all of which were used to assist the Northeast Volunteer Army. It was also decided to double the penalty, but the treacherous merchant ignored it and continued to traffic in enemy coal. Yesterday (the 23rd), the Anti-Japanese Association, based on Article 7 of the Regulations for Punishing Treacherous Merchants, sent personnel to seal up the coal shop and forced the treacherous merchant Wu Huangen into a rickshaw and paraded him through the streets as a warning to others. At noon that day, an emergency meeting was convened, ordering the treacherous merchant to sign a pledge and be photographed by the Anti-Japanese Association as a form of punishment.

Tan Ying Case Scheduled for Continued Hearing 88

The lawsuit involving Tan Ying and Gu Baosen was previously heard in the Suzhou Higher Court. At that time, Tan Ying's lawyer, Wang Jian, objected to Gu Baosen hiring a lawyer to appear in court. However, Gu Baosen's lawyers, Liu Zhen and Wang Peiyuan, argued that this case was a countersuit filed by the defendant Gu Baosen on the grounds of false accusation. Gu Baosen was the plaintiff in the countersuit, and according to the Criminal Procedure Law, he could appoint an agent, which was different from ordinary false accusations, which should be public prosecutions. This dispute was not resolved in court. It was then heard that Gu's lawyer, Liu Zhen, had also written a statement declaring that the appointment was indeed legal. It is now heard that the Higher Court has scheduled a continued hearing for February 2nd and has notified Gu's lawyer to appear in court. Furthermore, it is heard that the Higher Court has also investigated Tan Ying's age through the examination of her sachet, to aid in the investigation.

The Shanghai National Goods Traveling Promotion Group, in order to actively promote national goods and resist Japanese goods, has specially contacted local People's Education Centers to hold a large-scale national goods exhibition. Both Freighters and Civilian Boats Robbed Simultaneously 90

A freighter owned by boat owner Zou Axing was previously robbed at the San岔路口 intersection in Fangmatan, suffering heavy losses. On the afternoon of the 22nd, at 6 p.m., the freighter was traveling from Wuxi to Cheng as usual when it encountered three pirate ships. Twenty or thirty bandits jumped out, dressed in tattered military uniforms, each holding box cannons, pistols, and other weapons. They boarded the ship and robbed it, firing two shots as a warning. They robbed ten yuan in paper money from Yichang Money Shop in Beitang, this county, which was being sent to Zhao Xing Pawnshop in Yangku; nine foreign dollars sent by Wang Yusheng Rice Shop to Hemaochang; three hundred yuan in cash, three light bulbs, two small champagne cigarettes, five to six thousand steel yuan, two ginseng, a silver watch, and a cotton robe, belonging to Ye Linpei and being sent to Tong Shentang. The total loss was estimated to be over 1,000 yuan. At the same time, five civilian boats were also looted, with unspecified losses. After obtaining the stolen goods, the bandits jumped back onto their original ships and sped away in a southwest direction. Yesterday, freighter owner Zou Axing submitted a loss report to the Shipping Guild, which was forwarded to the county government for investigation.

Xiaoshan

Robbery Occurs in Dongzhuang Zhou 91

The household of Zhou Weisheng in Dongzhuang Zhou, outside the east gate of Xiaoshan, had some savings, and was coveted by bandits. On the night of the 21st, when the household was worshiping the gods, more than ten bandits suddenly arrived, each holding sharp blades and flashlights, and carried out a large-scale robbery. Two Boats Collide in the Dark Night 92

On the night of the 21st, a night boat from Shao to Xixing at Xiaoyang Bridge collided with a rice boat from Xiaoshan to Shao in the dark night. The boat sank instantly, and more than eighty bags of rice sank to the bottom of the river. Fortunately, there were few passengers on board, and they were rescued by Zou's boat, avoiding drowning. However, the boatman Amao died of exposure after being in the water for a long time.

Details of the Trip South 94

According to Qian, Mr. Duan Zhiquan is 69 years old and suffers from a foot ailment, making it difficult for him to move around. Therefore, he has been living in Tianjin for years, chanting scriptures and worshiping Buddha, and has not been involved in external affairs for a long time. This time, Chairman Chiang, considering the seriousness of the national crisis, recognized Mr. Duan as a veteran of our country who is very familiar with the situation in North China. Furthermore, Duan and Chiang have a teacher-student relationship. Therefore, Chairman Chiang urged Mr. Duan to go south to discuss national affairs together. Coincidentally, Qian was traveling to North China for matters related to the Four Banks Joint Reserve Depository. Chairman Chiang, upon hearing of this, telegraphed to Shanghai, instructing Qian to meet with him in Beijing and entrusted him with the task of welcoming Mr. Duan to the south, providing a handwritten letter to be presented to Mr. Duan. Qian arrived in Tianjin on the 19th and immediately visited Mr. Duan with Chairman Chiang's letter. Duan stated that at this time of jointly facing the national crisis, since the government has a comprehensive plan and approach to resist the enemy, people from all walks of life should unanimously support it. Although he is old, his patriotism is no less than anyone else's and he is willing to contribute his personal opinions on national salvation to the government as much as possible. Therefore, he resolutely went south on the 20th, arriving in Beijing yesterday (the day before yesterday). It was decided that today (yesterday) at 3 p.m., he would accompany Chairman Chiang to pay respects at the Mausoleum of Dr. Sun Yat-sen and take the night train to Shanghai that evening. He should arrive here tomorrow morning (this morning).

Mr. Duan met with Chairman Chiang twice in Beijing yesterday (the day before yesterday), and they had a very pleasant and in-depth conversation. Mr. Duan plans to rest in Shanghai for a few days, then go to Hangzhou and Putuo to worship Buddha, and then go to Qingdao to visit his second daughter, who is married to a Mr. Chen and works at the Qingdao branch of the Shanghai Bank. As for Mr. Duan's visit to Shanghai, Chairman Chiang has already telegraphed Mayor Wu, asking him to provide hospitality.

Zhang Ji Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday and Discusses Northwest Development 100

Our Country's Culture is Superior to Other Races

Aggressive Races Eventually Assimilate

The Chinese People Should Restore Their Self-Confidence

According to the Central News Agency, Central Committee member Zhang Puquan is about to go abroad because his eldest son and daughter are going to France to study. Therefore, he came south from Luoyang to bid farewell. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning and visited Mayor Wu at the Municipal Government at about 4 p.m. The reporter from the Central News Agency also happened to be visiting and had a long conversation. The details are as follows:

The Front is Spirited Zhang said that this time, the Japanese bandits attacked Yuguan, and the troops stationed there resisted with great spirit. Every time they heard orders, they competed to kill the enemy, showing excellent morale. Mr. Duan Zhiquan accepted Chairman Chiang's invitation to come south for discussions. This spirit of unity for the country is commendable. He also met General Wu Ziyu in Beijing, who expressed great indignation at the atrocities of neighboring Japan. He also stated that he would not leave Beijing for the time being and would never be used by others. If there was an opportunity, he would emulate Yue Wu Mu of the past and be loyal to the country. Therefore, various rumors about him from the outside world are not credible. This phenomenon is gratifying, but the people of the whole country must restore their self-confidence.

Glorious History Among those who have invaded our country in our history are the Liao, Jin, Yuan, and Qing dynasties. Although our country and people have been humiliated, they still admired our culture and were eventually assimilated by us. This fact is the glory of our national history and also the essence of our historical philosophy. The people of our country often boast that our country is the paradise of the world. Although this statement is an exaggeration, it is a manifestation of self-confidence. Now the self-confidence of the people of our country is gradually disappearing, and they even belittle themselves, feeling that they are inferior to others in everything. The crisis of the country and the nation lies in this. Our nation originated in Xi'an. When I traveled to Europe ten years ago, I saw the beauty of the cultures and the greatness of the nations. I always felt that it was an exaggeration for the people of our country to regard themselves as the paradise of the world. But this time when I traveled to Xi'an, I was able to admire the culture of the birthplace of our nation and its greatness. My self-confidence was restored. Xi'an and Luoyang are in the center of the country, and transportation is very convenient. The people of our country can go there for sightseeing and discover the beauty and greatness of our culture, and their self-confidence will be restored. Then there is no need to fear foreign enemies. Even if the country is humiliated, the nation will never be destroyed and may even assimilate foreign races.

Developing the Northwest Since Xi'an and Luoyang are the centers of our national culture, all construction is very important. It has been decided to establish Xi'an as a city, and the construction of Luoyang is also being planned. Luoyang is now designated as a cultural center, and the establishment of a branch of the Central Military Academy is actively underway. Ordinary education in the area is very good, while higher education is waiting for a planned development. Transportation to the area is very convenient. It only takes more than 20 hours to reach Luoyang from Shanghai. After the completion of the western section of the Longhai Railway, it will only take more than 20 hours to reach Xi'an. The people in the area are strong and simple. Although the area is still in the stage of agricultural economic development, the fertile land makes the people prosperous. The main products are cotton and small-scale handicrafts. If the people of our country can invest there, their development can be expected. Zhang said that Mayor Wu suggested organizing a Northwest Association to start with investigation and research and encourage people from Shanghai to go there for development. This proposal will soon become a reality, and the people of Shanghai will also be happy to assist.

Saving the Country with Science Zhang also said that the way to save the country is to seek substantive construction. Wu Zhihui's proposal to save the country with motors is a response to current malpractices. Education in China is now at the point of bankruptcy, and those responsible are theorists who advocate philosophy, literature, and dreamers who advocate world unity. Twenty years ago, when I met Mr. Wu in Europe, he advocated saving the country with science, saying that if everyone could wear a worker's hat, China could become strong. Twenty years later, his advocacy has not changed, but it has not been implemented, leading to the current situation. Therefore, I admire Mr. Wu. My children are going to France this time to enter industrial schools, hoping to become workers and return to China to contribute to the construction of the country.

Aviation for National Salvation Propaganda Week First Day 102

Mayor Wu Gave a Radio Speech Last Night

Only by Concentrating the Nation's Wisdom and Wealth Can We Build an Air Force

The Aviation for National Salvation Propaganda Week for all circles in this city was held for the first day yesterday. In addition to the meetings and speeches held separately by the municipal government's bureaus and departments and various groups, Mayor Wu Tiecheng also gave a radio speech at the Asia-America Radio Station at 7 p.m. The text of Wu's speech is recorded as follows:

Unprecedented Misfortune 103

In order to commemorate the January 28th Shanghai Incident of last year, the central government specially decided to designate this month from the 23rd to the 28th as Aviation Propaganda Week. The meaning of Aviation Propaganda Week is to enable the people of the whole country to deeply understand the importance of aviation for national salvation, and the Chinese nation can also, through the awakening of the people of the whole country and the completion of the construction of the air force, obtain a new opportunity for revival and self-strengthening. Today, I am undertaking the first radio speech elected by all circles, and I also want to announce this profound and important meaning to our dear compatriots across the country. The current stage of the Chinese nation, as everyone knows, has been deeply mired in unprecedented and serious misfortune. In the emotions of the general public, it has probably been felt that the beginning of this life-or-death national struggle can no longer be shirked or avoided. In fact, China's national crisis did not begin today, nor did it originate in the Northeast. Our Premier Sun, who cares about the fate of the country and loves the nation, had already told us in his speeches on nationalism, 'The position we are in now is a matter of life and death. The Chinese nation will soon perish. Summing up the disasters suffered by our nation, one is political oppression, the second is economic oppression, and the third is the oppression of the population increase of the great powers. These three major disasters from abroad have already arrived. Our nation is in a very dangerous position. For example, in terms of the first disaster, political power can destroy a country in one morning. China is now under the oppression of the political power of the great powers and can perish at any time. Today, we do not know the life and death of tomorrow because our navies, armies, and important places do not have national defense preparations. Foreign countries can rush in at any time and destroy China at any time. What is even more dangerous is that our peace-loving nation is still indifferent under this dangerous situation, unprepared, and even because 'soldiers are fierce and wars are dangerous,' everyone does not want martial force and dislikes military affairs to the extreme. This psychology and attitude of 'living in danger and stealing peace' and 'being afraid of breaking the vase while throwing a rock at the mouse' is really the greatest weakness in the national thinking. The greatest crisis of the Chinese nation, existing in heaven and earth, must have a foundation to stand on. If a country does not have a strong foundation, the nation will lose its life guarantee. 'In ancient times, the great affairs of the country were only sacrifice and war.' Even Confucius, who advocated benevolence and influence, recognized 'sufficient food and sufficient soldiers' as the basic principle for maintaining the life of the nation. If we cannot, under the principles of democracy, attempt to 'provide sufficient food' to support our nation, and under the principles of nationalism, attempt to 'provide sufficient soldiers' to protect our nation, then we will not only violate the Premier's profound teachings, but I am afraid we will have no way to survive in today's world of extremely acute national struggle."

Catch Up 104

If we want to continue the life of the nation under such a dangerous situation, we must first get rid of the long-standing psychology of depression and aversion to martial force, thoroughly recognize the difficulties of the nation's situation, bravely stand on the front line of the national struggle, enrich the nation's courage to fight, increase the nation's strength of self-defense, and exhaust the wisdom of the whole people to study national defense, exhaust the benevolence of the whole people to build national defense, and exhaust the courage of the whole people to strengthen national defense. However, national defense construction is not a matter of one day or two, especially given the breadth of our country's territory, the length of our coastline, and our coastal fortresses, either due to treaty oppression or due to financial constraints, have never had naval defenses along the coast. At the same time, in urban areas, especially in the cities of various provinces, there is no air defense equipment. Once the country is in trouble, it will be attacked from both inside and outside and cannot be defended. Under such an urgent situation, there is really no room for us to build leisurely, but there is a need to 'urgently rise up and catch up.' Now, the national defense plan to 'catch up' is air defense. In modern military affairs, based on the experiences of the European War and several wars in our country in recent years, air defense is the most economical, most effective, easiest to implement, and quickest national defense plan. Former military strategists regarded the coast as the first line of defense. Since the power of the air force has been revealed, coastal defense has lost its role, and the air force has become the center of modern national defense plans. Since air defense is economical, effective, and important, it is even more suitable and urgent for China, which has no foundation in national defense.

Importance of Air Defense 105

The air force is not only easy to organize and easy to see results, but also has the effect of preemptive strikes in military affairs, and its operational efficiency is unmatched by any navy or army. The art of war says, 'Know yourself and know your enemy, and you will win every battle.' Airplanes can scout the enemy's positions, take pictures of the locations of trenches, and explore the realities of enemy camps. Its ability to destroy enemy positions and shake military morale is particularly fierce. The people of the country can reflect on the Songhu campaign for proof. Therefore, French General Foch said, 'In the future Second World War, the most active and powerful will be airplanes.' The future combat formation must be a large-scale fleet of aircraft, galloping across the sky, and their destructive capabilities will far exceed those of the navy and army, causing the enemy country's military morale to collapse and disarm. Therefore, the future air force is the main driving force for the victory or defeat of war.

National Strengths 106

After the European War, countries, in view of the greatness of the air force, concentrated their national strength and financial resources to engage in air construction. According to the statistics of 1929, the air force equipment of various countries has made amazing progress, especially France. France has more than 40,000 air force personnel and more than 16,000 aircraft, followed by the United States, with 6,700 aircraft, and the United Kingdom also has more than 6,000 aircraft, with an air force budget of more than 20 million pounds. Russia has more than 4,000 aircraft, Italy has more than 3,000 aircraft, and Germany and Japan have about 2,000 aircraft. Japanese students also have air force military training, and their emphasis on the air force is particularly alarming. Other small countries, such as Poland and Spain, have more than 500 aircraft, and Switzerland and Belgium also have more than 400 aircraft. Looking around the world, only our great China is lagging behind in everything. The navy and army equipment are missing, and the air force equipment is not only almost zero in quantity compared with the great powers, but also only one-third or even one-half as fast. The speed of our country's airplanes is only more than 100 kilometers per hour, while other countries have 270 kilometers. The climbing power is about 3,000 meters in ten minutes. Flying in the air to fight like this, our planes are simply for the enemy to capture.

Concentrated Construction 107

Here, at this time, the people of our country should thoroughly recognize the horror of the world situation, recognize the dangers of the nation's situation, recognize the nation's urgent plan, bravely stand on the front line of the national struggle, enrich the nation's courage to fight, increase the nation's strength of self-defense, and know that air force construction is the center of modern national defense plans, air force construction is the plan to 'catch up' with national defense, air force construction is the most suitable for China, which is backward in military equipment, and air force construction is the most effective, easiest to implement, most economical, and most powerful national defense plan. Only by building an air force can we consolidate our national defense. Only by developing the air force can we save the nation from disaster. We must concentrate the wisdom of the whole country to build an air force and concentrate the wealth of the whole country to develop an air force.

Unity Can Resist Insults 108

Wu Tiecheng's Speech Mayor Wu Tiecheng presided over the memorial week held by the municipal government yesterday. After leading all the staff to perform the ceremony as usual, he gave a report. His words are as follows: There is an ancient saying in our country, 'Many hardships build a nation,' and also 'A country without external enemies often perishes.' Generally, a country that is full of hardships and humiliated is often able to make a tired and scattered nation alert and sensitive through stimulation, and unite through alertness and sensitivity. In the past hundred years, the oppression and threats from foreign countries have been incessant, and the people have gradually become alert and sensitive due to stimulation. Recently, the national crisis has become more urgent, and they have been able to gradually move towards unity through alertness and sensitivity. There have been many examples of this in our country, and the most gratifying thing is the arrival of Mr. Duan Zhiquan in the south. Mr. Duan created the Republic of China and maintained the country, which is admired by all. However, he has long been enjoying the tranquility of nature and has not heard of political affairs. Recently, he came to Beijing to discuss national affairs with the party and government leaders of the capital. This move is enough to set an example for the whole country, change the world's perception, and make people admire endlessly. He will be coming to Shanghai within days, and we should express our utmost respect and welcome to Mr. Duan's arrival, and we deeply believe that this sincere unity will have a great impact on the future of the country.

Zhang Zhijiang's Speech Zhang Zhijiang, the director of the Central Martial Arts Hall, told a reporter from the Central News Agency yesterday morning that his visit to Nanjing to see Chairman Chiang was specifically to contribute opinions and strategies on national defense. It is dangerous to resist foreign insults without solidifying national defense. The people must assist the government in carrying out solid national defense in order to achieve rapid results. If we rely solely on the government, we will inevitably be isolated and weak. Therefore, we deeply hope that the people of the country will work together with one heart to assist the government in resisting insults. The situation in North China is extremely dangerous. The only way to survive is to resist with force. There are many soldiers in North China, and we hope that the chief generals will do their best to plan everything and achieve the goal of recovering the lost territories. The art of war says, 'Who is the ruler who has the way, and who is the general who has the ability.' We deeply hope that Zhang Xueliang, the chief general of North China, will rejuvenate his spirit and insist on resistance. Feng Yuxiang is still residing in Zhangjiakou and is extremely indignant at the Japanese army's invasion. Therefore, he has repeatedly telegraphed to me to express his determination to kill the enemy. As for the rumor that General Feng is coming south, I have not heard of it.

Statement from the Postal Workers' Associations Regarding Minister Zhu's Remarks 118

According to yesterday's newspaper report on the remarks by Minister of Transportation Zhu Jia-hua regarding the reorganization of the post office, in order to maintain the domestic postal service, he has decided to immediately undertake streamlining, and all those who previously received salaries without working will be dismissed to save money. The local postal and postal worker associations claim that this situation does not exist in the post office. They telegraphed Minister Zhu on the same day, requesting a solemn statement to protect the reputation of postal personnel. The original telegram from the two associations is recorded below: "Nanjing Ministry of Transportation, Minister Zhu Jian, In today's newspaper reports, the Minister's remarks on the reorganization of the post office include the decision to immediately undertake streamlining in order to maintain the domestic postal service, and all those who previously received salaries without working will be dismissed to save money. Upon reading this, we were extremely surprised. The number of personnel used by the post office has always been based on the complexity of the tasks. Even when each postal area adds personnel, the reasons and the number of personnel to be added must be submitted to the higher authorities for approval before proceeding. This can be used as proof. Therefore, the phenomenon of receiving a salary without working is definitely not possible in the post office. Since the Minister took office, he has been very concerned about the benefits of the transportation industry, and the associations admire his initiatives for reform. However, since this matter has no factual basis, it is sufficient to confuse and mislead outsiders. We suspect that it was a mistake by the news reporter. As for the Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau, the employment and administration are different from the Postal Administration. Whether the above situation exists or whether the Minister's statement specifically refers to the Savings and Remittance Bureau, the associations have no way of knowing in detail. However, since it concerns the reputation of postal workers across the country, we hereby send a special telegram, requesting a solemn statement. We eagerly await your reply. Sincerely, Shanghai Postal Employees Union, Shanghai Postal Workers Union."

Laid-Off Workers of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Picketed Yesterday, Causing Disturbance 119

With the Protection of the Head Detectives, the Foremen Resolved the Situation at Dusk

The General Manager Received Them and Promised to Submit the Matter to the Board of Directors

According to the New Sound Society, the laid-off workers from the five wharves of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company continued to picket the Board of Directors yesterday afternoon at 2 PM to present their petition. However, because the directors were out, they did not achieve their goal, and a disturbance occurred. With the persuasion of the police, the situation was resolved by the General Manager's reception at dusk. The details are as follows:

Continued Petition The workers' union of the five wharves sent representatives Xue Yinkui, Fu Zhiyang, Li Angqing, Xue Xingbiao, Shan Xishou, Wu Jucai, Chen Shijun, Yu Xianting, and all the laid-off workers to the Board of Directors to present their petition at 2 PM yesterday afternoon. The standing directors were out, and Director Yang Zhixiong received them. The representatives demanded that they be reinstated or given one year's severance pay. Yang said that the matter was important and promised to notify the standing directors immediately for a reply. Therefore, all the petitioners waited in the auditorium.

Disturbance The Fourth Road General Police Station received a report and sent Chinese and foreign detectives to protect them. At 4 PM, Chinese foreman Jin Xinshan, Northern foreman He Tiehua, Southern foreman Li Yunsheng, Central foreman Fu Ruiquan, and New foreman Jin Yiru arrived at the Bureau one after another at the General Manager's call. All the laid-off workers questioned the foremen about the reasons for the layoffs, and the order was chaotic. Fortunately, the detectives stationed there dissuaded them, and the foremen took refuge in the General Manager's office. The laid-off workers guarded the front and back, it is said.

Visit to the General Manager After 5 PM, the laid-off workers asked General Manager Liu Hongsheng to notify the standing directors for a reply. The General Manager ordered the selection of representatives. The union sent Yu Xianting and the laid-off workers' representatives Fu Zhiyang and Shan Xishou to meet with him. At 5:35 PM, the five wharf foremen, He Tiehua and others, left the Bureau under the armed protection of police detectives. The union representatives presented a petition to the General Manager and detailed the truth about the corruption of the foremen and the unfairness of the layoffs. The General Manager promised to submit the petition to the Board of Directors for consideration and then decide on a fair solution and reply. They did not disperse until 8 PM.

Evening General Assembly All the laid-off workers felt that the petition had no practical solution and immediately lined up and returned to the Fifth Wharf Union. They held an emergency general assembly to discuss the final plan. Yu Xianting reported on the process first. Yu believed that the General Manager's reply was not satisfactory, and it was decided to continue to expand the petition to the Board of Directors on the 24th until the goal was achieved.

Maritime Students In the second layoff of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, all twelve graduates of the first class of the Maritime Specialty School established by the company were laid off. It is reported that the students submitted a petition to the Board of Directors of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and General Manager Liu yesterday, requesting them to withdraw the order and complete their studies.

Japanese Government Subsidizes Nisshin Steamship Company's Shipping Costs 120

The Nisshin Steamship Company's business in China is mainly on the Yangtze River, supplemented by North and South Ocean liners. Since the January 28th Incident last year, boycotts of Japanese ships have occurred everywhere, and the Nisshin River and Sea shipping business has plummeted. Currently, only four ships are operating on the Yangtze River, one ship is operating upstream, and more than a dozen ships are empty and moored in Shanghai. The Nanhua class business is even quieter, only sailing to Hong Kong. The company's business losses last year were huge. Now, the Japanese government's Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Navy are subsidizing all the company's expenses, so the company has been ordered to operate as usual and wait for the opportunity to develop. Therefore, the decline in business has nothing to do with the company itself.

The Family Toothbrush Factory on National Goods Road suspended work earlier due to a shortage of raw materials.
