An agreement was reached immediately.

Taxpayers' Association Sends Letter to the Public Works Department Requesting Not to Overestimate Rent to Collect Donations 126

Financial Management Must Consider Legality and Facts

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession sent a letter to the Public Works Department yesterday, stating: "Sir, according to a letter from the First Branch of the Shanghai Citizens' Federation, our member, Yile Tian Teahouse at 513 Nanjing Road, and its affiliated Tong Yu Chun Teahouse at 463 Nanjing Road, stated that they received notices from the Public Works Department on December 23rd last year, informing our Yile Tian Teahouse that the annual house donation, which was previously 4,000 yuan, must be increased to 9,240 yuan from April 1st, and our affiliated Tong Yu Chun Teahouse, which paid 4,400 yuan, must be increased to 6,240 yuan, which is more than twice and one-third of the original amount. However, upon investigation, our teahouse and affiliated teahouse have been operating on Nanjing Road for more than ten years. The house donation has always been based on the rent ticket. Now, the Public Works Department is forcibly estimating the price, treating the rent of old houses as the expensive rent of newly renovated houses, which is unfair in principle. Moreover, our teahouse's business is light and profitable, and we usually make ends meet with copper coins. Since the January 28th Incident, our business has plummeted. If we are suddenly asked to increase the donation, it will be even more difficult to bear. We earnestly request your association to forward a letter to the Public Works Department, asking them to understand the difficulties of businesses and continue to collect donations according to the original amount, and to forward a request to the Citizens' General Association and the Chinese Taxpayers' Association to provide consistent assistance, etc. Accordingly, the number of house donations is calculated based on the amount of rent, which is an immutable principle. If the Public Works Department wants to increase revenue and forcibly overestimate the rent in order to collect more donations, it is directly oppressive to the people and indirectly encourages landlords to increase rent prices, which hides the motive for the society to become increasingly insecure. This violates the Public Works Department's duty to maintain law and order. From the standpoint of a taxpayer, we cannot recognize the oppressive policy of estimating prices to collect donations, not only for businesses that are struggling to survive, but also in the state of paying donations according to the law. According to the previous letter, it is appropriate to request your association to forward a letter to the Public Works Department, requesting that the house donations for Yile Tian and Tong Yu Chun should always be collected according to the original amount, and to stop similar administrative actions from being applied to any taxpayer in order to maintain social security and benefit citizens' businesses, etc. Upon approval of this, this case, in terms of legality, has a municipal general donation based on actual rent as a standard. It is absolutely impossible to overestimate the rent to increase revenue and increase the burden on taxpayers. Your Bureau also agrees with this principle, so it has punished a certain number on Shanxi Road for forging rent tickets. In terms of facts, the total donation of Yile Tian per year must be increased by 131%, from 4,000 yuan to 9,240 yuan, and Tong Yu Chun must be increased by 40%, from 4,400 yuan to 6,200 yuan. The two teahouses are commercial institutions, and their business has a certain limit on expenses. How can it suddenly swell? The national and local governments must also determine the method based on the presence or absence or increase or decrease of the tax source if they want to increase revenue and balance the budget. May I ask if there is a civil servant whose income is fixed? Suppose a certain expenditure of his suddenly increases by one or one-third above the previous level, how will he make up for his personal budget? Or it may be said that he can obtain a salary increase or subsidy from the public office to make up for it. This is indeed the current situation. However, suppose that under the difficult environment of public offices, various commercial and industrial enterprises cannot maintain themselves, and therefore go bankrupt and close down, resulting in a large number of unemployed, and public security is worrying, the cost of defense increases. At the same time, new houses such as the Jardine Matheson & Co. in the Public Concession are not sought after, and old houses continue to be vacated. The revenue from general donations decreases, and even falls into the same plight as the depleted municipal finances of Chicago in the United States. What method will he use to obtain a salary increase or subsidy to make up for his insufficient personal budget? I am taking this opportunity to ask your Bureau to urgently formulate a financial policy to cope with the current situation: ㈠ Taxpayers and those who serve taxpayers should commonly endure the pain of economic depression. ㈡ Except for the costs of maintaining public security and improving citizens' intelligence, either reduce or even eliminate them. This association believes that Shanghai's business must rely on the purchasing power of the interior of the Yangtze River basin, which is almost equal to zero due to the Japanese disturbances, the preciousness of gold and the cheapness of silver, the floods in seven provinces, and the reason for the low price of shells harming farmers. Shanghai's commercial and industrial enterprises are all in a state of frugality and hardship. If donations and taxes are increased, and rents are increased again due to estimates, once the tenuous financial line is lost, the number of vacant houses will increase day by day, and the tax source will decrease day by day. At that time, the financial situation of your Bureau will be unknown. This association is deeply concerned. According to the previous letter, it is appropriate to request your Bureau to carefully consider the law and facts in handling financial affairs. Sincerely, The Shanghai Public Concession Public Works Department."

Shui Mingchang Proposes Solution to Water Bill Issue 131

｜Real Estate Association Responds to Pay at Old Rate｜

Shui Mingchang, a member of the Real Estate Association and manager of an accounting firm, yesterday exchanged letters with the Real Estate Association regarding the case of water bills being five times higher after the installation of water meters. The letters are as follows: (Letter from Shui Mingchang) Respectfully, I have just received a water bill from the water company for the period from December 1st to December 16th, totaling $98.75. Upon investigation, based on the fixed water rate, the monthly water bill should be $38.43. Compared to the past, this is an increase of more than five times. Based on reason and fact, it is impossible to pay accordingly. In addition to sending a letter to the water company to protest, I am writing to your association to strongly advocate on our behalf to the water company to avoid unexpected losses. Regarding the water bill, should we delay payment, or pay according to the fixed water rate? I request your association to be responsible for guiding us. Upon investigation, this case has been delayed for many days, and we have no idea how to deal with the water company. If this continues, it will be endless. Based on my members' opinions, I propose the following: (1) Request the water company to install water meters for each tenant, and all methods should follow the methods of the power company. It would be unreasonable for landlords to pay for deposits and water meters, and we should firmly refuse to the end. (2) Request the water company to continue charging the fixed water rate, or add one, for each room with a rent of $30 or $50 or less, and not change the original agreement to avoid disputes. (3) If your association does not have a proper solution, you must inform each member to find their own solutions. (Reply from the Real Estate Association) Respectfully replying, we have received your letter of January 20th regarding the increase in water bills by five times after calculation by water meter. We understand everything. The two methods you proposed are very appropriate and have already been incorporated into previous statements. As for the payment method, since it is not yet formal, you can pay at the old rate pending a solution. A tripartite meeting will be held soon.

Muslims Held Grand Prayers Last Night 132

This month is the Muslim holy month of Ramadan. Muslims fast during the day, abstaining from food and drink, and break their fast at night before eating. Yesterday was the "Eid al-Fitr" (translated phonetically) evening of Ramadan. All mosques in Shanghai held grand prayer ceremonies last night. All Muslims went to the mosques to pray. Each mosque set up temporary sheds in the courtyards to alleviate overcrowding.

An Old Villager Shot and Killed 135

Yin Afu, a farmer from Xiaoliujiazhai in Baoshan County, had some savings. He recently received a threatening letter stating that "the end of the year is difficult to pass," demanding $1,200, otherwise they would take drastic measures. It was arranged that the money should be sent by someone carrying a vegetable basket to the Shuimenjiang Bridge near Sanguantang in Songbei on the afternoon of the previous day, where someone would collect it. Yin was terrified after receiving the letter because he had no such large sum of money. If he refused, his life would be in danger. He had no choice but to report to the Baoshan County Security Corps. After receiving the report, Director Yan ordered the corps members to disguise themselves as scheduled and go to the agreed location to lie in ambush. At about 4 PM on the previous day, the corps dispatched the squad leader leading many corps members to disguise themselves and wait. They deliberately placed a vegetable basket on the ground. At that time, a villager dressed person passed by and frequently asked the corps members how to get to Yuepu, while staring at the vegetable basket on the ground. The corps members suspected that his appearance was suspicious and tried to arrest him. The villager suddenly reached into his arms. Squad Leader Zhang suspected that he was reaching for a weapon and quickly fired a box cannon at him. The bullet hit his waist, and he fell to the ground and died. It is difficult to determine whether this person was a bandit. Yesterday, the corps director reported to the county government, and County Chief Jin sent officials to the scene for inspection in the morning. The inspection revealed that the deceased was nearly sixty years old, with slightly gray hair, wearing a cloth cotton robe and a blue cloth bamboo skirt. He had two pieces of salted meat on his back. There were no weapons beside him. There were several dollars in his pocket. The bullet entered from the waist and exited from the chest, causing death. Currently, no relatives have claimed the body, and the local bailiff will collect it.

Four Examinations of Wife's Virginity, Deemed a Major Insult 136

Court Grants Divorce of Song Tianxiang and Tu Fumei

Song Ordered to Compensate for Losses and Pay Alimony, Etc.

Song Tianxiang, a doctor from Ningbo, married Tu Fumei, a woman from the same town, as his second wife in the winter of the year before last. After the marriage, he repeatedly forced Tu to undergo examinations at Tongde, Fumin, and other hospitals, up to four times, claiming that she was not a virgin. However, the examination results could not determine that she was not a virgin. Since then, Song has abused her, causing her to feel unable to live with him. She hired lawyer Wu Peng to file a lawsuit for divorce and requested the court to order the defendant to compensate for losses, alimony, and dowry. Song also filed a counterclaim, stating that if they were to divorce, Tu should compensate for the marriage expenses. After repeated hearings by the First Special District Court, lasting almost a year, Judge Luo Chongtai announced the verdict yesterday morning, ordering the defendant Song Tianxiang to divorce Tu Fumei, and to compensate for losses of $440, pay alimony of $2,000, and return all of the plaintiff's dowry, or compensate $600 for the dowry. The plaintiff was responsible for nine-tenths of the litigation costs, and the defendant was responsible for one-tenth. The plaintiff's other claims and the defendant's counterclaim were dismissed. The costs of the counterclaim were borne by the counterclaimant. After the judgment, Judge Luo briefly stated the main points of the judgment, saying that the plaintiff left home because she could not live with the defendant, and had been away for one year and ten months. The minimum living expenses per month are $20, and based on this calculation, the defendant should compensate the plaintiff $440. As for the plaintiff's claim for alimony of $18,000, the amount is excessive. However, the defendant forced the plaintiff to undergo examinations for virginity up to four times, which must be regarded as a major insult. Therefore, considering the defendant's ability, he was ordered to pay $2,000, which is only one-tenth of what the plaintiff requested. Therefore, the defendant is also responsible for one-tenth of the litigation costs. Regarding the return of the dowry, the list opened by the plaintiff is exaggerated, but according to the testimony of witnesses, it can be known that there are indeed items worth six to seven hundred dollars. If the defendant fails to return the original items, he should compensate $600.

Notice of Business Vessels' Suspension During Year-End Closing 137

Various shipping companies in Shanghai have agreed to suspend sailings for a few days, at most one week and at least three days, during the year-end closing period. To facilitate travel for everyone, the reporter has compiled the suspension dates of various routes, as follows:

Shanghai-Ningbo - The Ningbo route has two ships departing every day. The four companies have agreed on the suspension dates for the end of the lunar year and the beginning of the year: (1) The Ningshao Company's Xin Ningshao ship will depart from Shanghai to Ningbo today, then dock in Ningbo, and return from Ningbo on the 28th, resuming service in Shanghai on the 29th. (2) The Sanbei Ningxing ship is being repaired and replaced by the Xin Ningxing. It is scheduled to depart for Ningbo today, then dock in Ningbo. It will also depart from Ningbo on the 28th, returning to Shanghai and resuming service on the 29th. (3) The Taikoo Xin Beijing ship will dock in Shanghai on the 25th and suspend service for six days, resuming service on the 31st. (4) The China Merchants New Jiangtian ship will arrive in Shanghai on the 26th and suspend service for two days, departing on the 28th.

Tongyang - The Shanghai-Tongyang route is operated by Dada and Datong companies. Yesterday, Datong Shipping Bureau suspended service first, agreeing to suspend service for one week and resume service on the 30th. Dada Shipping Company has also planned to suspend service for six days starting today, resuming service on the 29th.

Shanghai-Taiwan - The six shipping companies on the Shanghai-Taiwan route are jointly ordered by the Lian An Shipping Bureau to suspend sailings during the year-end closing period. It has been agreed that the six ships will suspend service according to their schedules. Ping An Dahua has already stopped sailing from yesterday. The remaining ships will gradually dock in Shanghai and stop service, each suspending service for one week and resuming service from the 31st. All passengers have been notified.

Inland Rivers - There are more than a dozen inland river steamships in Shanghai, operating within Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. They have agreed to begin suspending sailings from the 25th and 26th, for three or four days. In addition, all regular Yangshang ships on the Yangtze River route will not suspend service, even if they are empty. However, due to the continuous drop in river water levels in recent days, many Jianglun ships entering the port have been delayed.

Stoker Died Tragically from Coal Gas Poisoning Due to Poor Ventilation of Coal Stove 139

｜Pay Attention to Those Burning Coal for Heating｜

Zhu Lairong, a 24-year-old from Tongzhou, worked as a stoker at the Luochang Construction Factory at 550 West Huade Road. The night before, Zhu, suffering from the cold, took a coal stove, burned coal in it, and placed it in his bedroom to provide heat. Then he closed the door and went to sleep alone. Unexpectedly, while Zhu was asleep, the coal gas could not escape, causing coal gas poisoning and loss of consciousness. The next day, Teng Lansheng, the head of the factory, went to see that the door was tightly closed and called out without response. Realizing that something was wrong, he found a way to open the door and saw Zhu collapsed on the bed. He immediately reported to the Huishan Police Station and ordered detectives to investigate. Zhu was taken by car to Tongren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died soon after. The body was taken to the Philander Road Corpse Examination Office. Yesterday morning, he reported to the First Special District Court and commissioned Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, to inspect the body. During the public investigation, Teng Lansheng testified that when he walked into the deceased's bedroom, he saw that there were still embers in the coal stove and felt a strong coal gas smell in the room. At that time, the deceased was already unconscious, so he reported to the police station. Zhu Renrong, the deceased's younger brother, also testified. Guo determined that Zhu Lairong died of coal poisoning and ordered the corpse to be handed over to his younger brother Zhu Renrong to take back for burial.

Yangzhou Prostitute Ling Kidnaps Two Beauties to Shanghai 140

A Pair of Sisters Were Both Kidnapped and Raped

Prostitute Ling Yao Ji Spreads Through Yangzhou City

Elder Sister Already Married, Younger Sister Speaks Freely of Love

All Three are Detained Pending Transfer of Documents

Feng Junrui from Jiangdu County Yangzhou First Stage, a Wu Sheng from Anhui, is quite talented and handsome, and young. Many women in the county with romantic tendencies have been seduced by him. The Bian family in the town is a prominent family in Weiyang, with Bian Shuluan and Bian Zhenhui. The two are sisters. Shuluan and Feng are the same age, thirty-nine years old, and have already been married. Zhenhui is twenty-nine years old and waiting to be married, currently studying at a certain school in Yangzhou. She is beautiful and takes a bus to the First Stage in her free time to listen to music. Her father has passed away for many years, and her widowed mother dotes on her and does not restrain her, so her presence is almost daily in the theater. If her older sister Shuluan returns to Ning, she will take her along. Over time, this pair of sisters became noticed by Ling Feng, and the sisters also felt that the Ling Feng was handsome and young and worthy of a lover. So, they actually practiced the act of secret trysts. Ling Feng's wish to have a double pleasure was also fulfilled. Although they were all secret affairs, it was difficult to keep the truth from being revealed. Thus, rumors spread and gradually reached the ears of the two beauties' families. It was said that they were prostituting and it became difficult to tolerate, so Ling Feng persuaded the Bian sisters to each roll up their clothes and escape together. The woman's mother reported to the Jiangdu County Public Security Bureau after the fact and requested an investigation. The bureau suspected that they might have fled to Shanghai, where people from all walks of life gather, so they sent detective Ju Hao with an arrest warrant to Shanghai to investigate their whereabouts. At 4:00 PM the day before yesterday, it was discovered that Ling Feng was enjoying tea at the Xiyuan Tea House at the intersection of Chongqing Road and Dagu Road in Xinzha. He immediately informed the Chinese police at No. 2441 of the nearby Mingtong and went to the tea house to arrest Ling Feng and take him to the Xinzha Police Station. Under interrogation, it was revealed that the Bian sisters were hiding at No. 16 Caishi Street in the French Concession. The police chief then sent detectives Liu Longchao and requested assistance from the French police to arrest the two women. Yesterday morning, they were taken to the First Special District Court. Judge Qian Wenzhong interrogated them. The Jiangdu detective Ju Hao requested that Feng and others be taken back to Yangzhou for questioning, but the police lawyer Wang Yaotang said that the detective was carrying an arrest warrant. If he wanted to transfer them, he should ask the detective to obtain a formal document from the Yangzhou authorities, so the case was requested to be postponed. Bian Zhenhui confessed that because her mother wanted to marry her to her brother-in-law as a concubine, which was not only not what she wanted, but also not wanted by her sister, she agreed with her sister to come to Shanghai with Feng. This was not her initiative, and she loved him. She spoke eloquently and without any shyness. She was even more beautiful than her sister. It is said that Ling Feng's acquisition of these two beauties, if not obtained by seduction, would be a truly great fortune. Currently, Feng and others are still temporarily detained, pending the arrival of documents from Jiangdu for verification.

Police Officer Ten Fires Shot, Mistakenly Kills Noodle Shop Owner 141

Caused by Association Disputes

A Life is Lost for Nothing

Zhou Ronggui, the 28-year-old owner of the Zhou Wanxing Noodle Shop in Qinglong Bridge, Nanshi, was from Danyang. His deceased brother had a six-dollar association share with Jiang Boxian of Xing Juli No. 12 Nanhui Hall Road. After his brother's death, his sister-in-law remarried, but she declared to Jiang that her brother-in-law should not take the association money, otherwise she would not recognize it. Unexpectedly, at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday (22nd), Zhou Ronggui went to the association stall and won the association share. Jiang refused to hand it over because his sister-in-law had said so, and told him that if he wanted to take the money, he had to find a guarantor. Zhou agreed and left. At 6:30 PM, he came again. According to Jiang Boxian, Zhou gathered two Jiangbei thugs, one of whom had a gun. He was having dinner at the time and was threatened with a gun, forcing him to take more than 140 dollars from his pocket. However, while the two sides were arguing, Jiang's wife ran outside and reported to the police that there was a robbery with a gun, and that there were guns, etc. Liu Lindong, a winter defense policeman on duty in Zone One, Substation One, came with his rifle. After receiving the report, he rushed into the house with his gun. The so-called two Jiangbei thugs had disappeared. Only Zhou Ronggui was still in the house, being held by Jiang, who was pulling on his long clothes. The police officer entered the room, and Zhou tore his clothes and broke free, escaping out of the door. The police officer shouted to stop him. Zhou rushed out, and his hand seemed to be raised upwards. The police officer immediately thought it was resistance and aimed, shooting Zhou in the head. The bullet hit his left cheekbone, exited from the left brain, and the hole was as big as a bowl. Brain matter flowed out, and he immediately fell dead in the courtyard. The police officer shone a flashlight on him and realized that he was an acquaintance. At that time, the security corps gathered and sent Jiang and his wife and the police officer to Zone One, Substation One. After interrogation by Section Chief Yi, they were immediately transferred to the Public Security Bureau yesterday morning and then transferred to the District Court for verification. Qin Defang, the land bailiff of the Twenty-third Shop, was ordered to report to the hospital for examination. Prosecutor Yang and others were commissioned to inspect the scene and ordered the corpse to be collected, pending strict interrogation and thorough investigation.

Sincere Amusement Park Homicide Verdict 143

Meng Lanting Sentenced to Ten Years for Murder

Zhang Yanxia, a Kunqu opera singer at the Sincere Amusement Park on Nanjing Road, was originally acquainted with Meng Lanting, a painter who drew scenery for the amusement park. Later, she disliked Meng's age and became deeply involved with Zhang Agao, a young rogue, even practicing the principle of "subsidizing" him, leading to the pawning of all her possessions. However, Zhang Agao's desires were insatiable. On account of the singer, he frequently demanded money from Meng Lanting for his extravagant spending. At 3:30 PM on the 10th of this month, Zhang suddenly broke into Meng's studio to borrow money. Unable to get it, they clashed. Zhang injured Meng's arm, and Meng immediately grabbed a hatchet and repeatedly struck Zhang's head and other parts of his body, causing him to fall to the ground. Zhang was quickly sent to the hospital by the police, but due to the fatal injuries, he soon died. Meng and Zhang Yanxia were detained and sent to the First Special District Court. After interrogation, the court found that Zhang, the singer, was not involved and ordered her immediate release. Meng Lanting was detained for further investigation. Details of these events have been reported in this newspaper. Now, Meng has been prosecuted for murder. The criminal court of the court, presided over by Judge Qian Wenji, repeatedly summoned witnesses and concluded the investigation. Yesterday morning was the sentencing date. Police lawyer Ru Bao Yi and the defendant's defense lawyer Fan Gang appeared in court as scheduled. At 9:00 AM, Judge Qian ascended the bench and ordered the defendant to be sentenced. Meng Lanting was found guilty of murder and sentenced to ten years of imprisonment. After the sentence was pronounced, Meng was taken back to the police station by the police to await confirmation and then be sent to prison to serve his sentence.

Robbery on Xinjiang Road: Two Robbers Caught 144

At 12:30 PM yesterday, a robbery occurred at No. 6 Dazheng Lane, Xinjiang Road, Zhabei. When the victim, Zhang Meigang, was having lunch with his family, five robbers suddenly arrived outside the door. Only one of the robbers had a gun. After knocking on the door and entering, they threatened the family, forbidding them from making any noise. The armed robber locked everyone in the house in the back room to watch over them, while the remaining robbers rushed upstairs, ransacking boxes and chests, and searching each room. After about an hour, they escaped with their loot. At this time, the victim saw that the robbers had fled, so he rushed out and saw one of the robbers still walking in front. He followed him secretly until near the Pot Lane intersection of Nanjing Road and Jiangxi Road. Seeing three or four Chinese police officers patrolling, the victim immediately went up and reported the crime. The police quickly caught up and arrested two robbers, seizing the stolen goods and two pistols from them. They were taken to the police station. Under interrogation by the police chief, the two identified themselves as Li Changsheng, from Pudong, 28 years old, and Zhou Heshang, from Yangzhou, 25 years old. However, the location of the crime was in the Fourth District, and the victim reported the case to the Fourth District Office. Later, they sent officers to transfer the case to the police station to investigate and arrest the accomplices before further processing the case. The victim's losses included a pair of pearl bracelets, a pair of gold bracelets, a gold watch, a gold ring, a fox fur coat, and 95 yuan in cash, totaling over a thousand yuan.

World chess champion Alekhine will arrive in Shanghai today on the President Taft. He is expected to stay for a week. Prostitute and Dancer in Mutual Assault Lawsuit 146

Bixia had a sister in the same profession, Zhang Meimei (16 years old), a Shanghai woman who worked as a dancer at the Yue Gong dance hall and also lived with Bixia. The reason was that on the 3rd of this month, Zhang Meimei first insulted the plaintiff, and then Bixia directed the assault, injuring Hua's arms and other parts of her body. Hua resisted slightly, and then the defendants falsely accused her of assault and robbery, leading to her being fined. At the time, the plaintiff also stated that she was injured in the assault, but the court stated that the police had not reported it and instructed her to file a separate lawsuit, which is why she filed the complaint. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhao Linyu of the First Special Court's Criminal Division summoned the defendants Bixia and Zhang Meimei, who also hired lawyer Yu Jun to defend them. Tens of Starved and Frozen to Death Daily

Report on Winter Relief in War-Torn Areas of This City 148

The China Jisheng Society, the United Xinwei Relief Society, and the Moral General Society jointly organized winter relief in the war-torn areas. They received 278 bags of relief rice and 2,000 yuan from the Xinwei Relief Society, 5,000 yuan from the Moral Society, and 42 shi and 7 dou of relief rice from the Wusong Municipal Committee Office. The rest was allocated and distributed by the Jisheng Society itself. Mr. Zhang Junxian was publicly elected as the director, and along with relief workers Li Yunmen, Gu Yabin, and others, they conducted daily on-site investigations in the severe winter wind and snow. They distributed to over 880 extremely poor households in Dachang and the east of the railway, spending 3,228 yuan. The war trenches in that area were filled, and labor relief and repairs were made to one road bridge and two other bridges, spending 1,800 yuan, 100 bags of rice, and 150 sets of cotton clothing. They distributed to over 1,420 households in the four villages of Jiangwan and the town, spending 9,128 yuan and 200 sets of cotton clothing. They distributed to over 1,190 households in the four villages of Wusong and the town, spending 5,271 yuan, 100 bags of rice, and another 42 shi and 7 dou, 500 sets of cotton clothing, and 50 cotton quilts. The remaining 78 bags of rice were handed over by the Jisheng Society to Mr. Wang Binyan of the Zhabei Charity Group for distribution. In total, Zhabei winter relief spent over 19,480 yuan, 178 bags of rice, another 42 shi and 7 dou, 850 sets of relief clothing, and 50 cotton quilts. The disaster situation in each area is extremely widespread, and disaster victims are crying out for help. At this time of harsh winter weather, they are suffering from both hunger and cold, making it difficult to reach everyone. With limited resources and many in need, we are truly ashamed to say that we have done little to help.

Development of New Shipping Route at Doulong Port 149

Establishment of Large-Scale Salt Warehouses

Jiangbei's Yancheng and Funing are salt-producing areas. Salt is traditionally transported to Hunan and Hubei, which requires transfer to ships at Haizhou, incurring huge costs. Now, Finance Minister Song Ziwen plans to establish a large-scale salt warehouse near the coastal areas of Haizhou, Yancheng, and Funing to centralize the production and sales of salt in the Yancheng and Funing areas. The warehouse will be able to hold 200,000 to 300,000 tons of Huai salt. The Ministry of Finance has appointed specialists to conduct on-site surveys in the Yancheng and Funing areas. The results indicate that Doulong Port, located north of the Sheyang River and inside Xinyang Port and Yaosha, is a good harbor area that does not freeze in winter and has deep water. It is close to Xiaogang Town, making it a convenient route for transporting salt produced in Yancheng and Funing. After the survey, it was decided to build the largest salt warehouse in the Huai area, sufficient for storing 300,000 tons of salt. The materials for building the warehouse have been purchased from Europe and America. The three items of hardware, cement, and wood alone total 50,000 tons and have already been shipped to Shanghai. As the salt warehouse is about to start construction, these materials will be transported by China Merchants Steam Navigation Company (CMSNC) ships. When the salt warehouse is built, a new shipping route will be opened at Doulong Port. Discussions have been held with CMSNC to add Shanghai-Doulong Port liners. CMSNC has instructed Shen Zhiyou, the special commissioner in Haizhou, to investigate the water depth in the area to facilitate ship operation and transport of the large batch of warehouse materials.

Divorce Lawsuit of "Spring Dreams in the Old Capital" Actress Sang Shuzhen 152

Zhang Bin, courtesy name Yaosheng, from Minhang Town in Shanghai County, is the son of Zhang Yunxi, the owner of Zhang Yimao Rice Shop in North Street, Minhang, and possesses considerable wealth. After graduating from Peking National University in Peiping in his early years, Zhang worked in the Ministry of Communications. Later, he was transferred to the Shanghai Telecommunications Section of the Ministry of the Navy, and then to the Ministry of the Navy. He currently serves as a telecommunications engineer in the Jiangsu Provincial Construction Department. He is very busy with public affairs and earns a good income. During the first year of the Xuantong era of the Qing Dynasty, Zhang met Sang Xiuying (currently 45 years old), a respectable woman from Changshu, Suzhou, who was 21 years old at the time. She was studying at the Jinghai Women's School in Suzhou. She was intelligent and skilled in poetry and prose, and both her parents had passed away. Zhang and Sang became acquainted, and their friendship developed into marital love. They married in Zhang's home in Minhang in the first year of the Republic of China, and their marital relationship was very close. However, they had no children. Years ago, when Zhang was in Peiping, he fell in love with a woman and had a son named Zhaozhong, whom he brought back and handed over to Sang to raise. Zhaozhong is now 16 years old and is taught at home by Sang. Unexpectedly, around 1926, Zhang suddenly changed and married a concubine, a woman from Wuxi named Lu, who is 31 years old this year. Lu lives with Sang in No. 11 Yongyu Lane, Belle Road, French Concession. When Zhang married the concubine, he asked someone to mediate with Sang, and the two parties agreed on four terms. Later, the wife and concubine inevitably became jealous of each other, causing Zhang and Sang's marital love to break down from then on. Zhang stopped paying Sang's monthly expenses and ignored her livelihood. Sang's appeals were ineffective and met with disdain. At this point, Sang, unable to bear the suffering, took her son and moved out, renting a room in the pavilion on the first floor of No. 9 Guifu Lane, Baille Road, Taiping Bridge. She has been over-pawning her belongings. Last year, due to financial difficulties, she joined the Lianhua Film Company as a supporting actress in the sequel "Spring Dreams in the Old Capital," playing the role of Sang Shuzhen, which is Sang's alias. Recently, she has been living in sorrow, while Zhang and his concubine Lu reside in Zhenjiang, neglecting her. This situation cannot continue for long. Realizing that her strength is gradually declining and she will be unable to earn a living, she has no choice but to hire lawyer Zhu Dianqing to represent her in filing a petition with the Civil Division of the Second Special District Court, requesting a divorce from Zhang and Lu, ordering them to pay alimony and education expenses for her son, totaling 29,500 yuan, and returning the seized items. The court has accepted the petition and issued summonses to be delivered to both parties, scheduling a mediation hearing for 2:00 PM on the 31st of this month.

Reader's Advisor

Issues of Worker Life and Self-Study 161

| Letter from Liang Jun |

I am twenty years old this year, and I am confident in my strong physique. Three years ago, I graduated from junior middle school, but due to my poor family circumstances, I had to drop out of school. Through a friend's introduction, I got a job in an agency, where I spend all day copying documents and enduring the faces of others. I work for over ten hours a day and manage to earn thirty yuan a month. However, my parents, younger brother, and younger sister make a total of five people in my family. With my elderly father and young siblings, the entire family's livelihood depends on my shoulders. No matter how frugal we are, we always feel that our expenses are not covered. If an unexpected event occurs, it would be even harder to cope. I am inherently unwilling to beg for pity from others, and now I often think about finding some side jobs to do—I have time in the mornings to help people with copying or bookkeeping—but I lack connections. I also plan to save one or two yuan from my allowance each month to prepare for emergencies, but in reality, it is difficult to implement. Looking ahead, how am I supposed to cope with this livelihood problem? Secondly, my profession, as mentioned above, is a clerk's life, which I often feel is not suited to my personality. The hardship of the work is worse than that of cattle and horses, and I am often looked down upon. If I quit, given the circumstances of my family, where would I go to find food? I know that this is all due to a lack of specialized skills and academic experience. Therefore, I am now eager to learn some specialized skills and knowledge, such as accounting, bookkeeping, surveying, etc.—but I am limited by my working hours and financial capabilities, so it is difficult to achieve my wishes. Moreover, there are very few people now who can truly teach me practical skills, and even if there are tutorial schools, I dare not try them lightly! How can this be remedied?

Answer: Your letter raises two questions, but in reality, it is just the overall structure of the social economy. However, our answer will be divided into the following three items: ㈠ Worker treatment issues. In the current social organization, class distinctions are extremely strict. The abuse of lower-level workers by upper-level personnel is a very common phenomenon. If you still hope to find better treatment than others in the various agencies of this vast urban society, that is an illusion, because all crows are generally black. This is not a moral issue, but an entire economic issue, an entire social issue. It is best to: on the one hand, temporarily endure and continue working; on the other hand, workers should unite and seek ways to improve the situation. If your vision is only focused on yourself and your family, you will never turn around. ㈡ Family life issues. How can a young junior middle school graduate like you bear the burden of a family of five? It is truly pitiful. This will naturally not be a problem in a country with future social changes, or in a society after the elimination of the state; because in such a society, the education of all children of workers, peasants, and the poor should be borne by society, and the old, weak, orphaned, disabled, and sick should be supported by society. However, in China, and even in the highly developed capitalist countries of Europe and America, this level cannot be achieved. Not only can this level not be achieved, but on the one hand, wealth is being created day by day, and on the other hand, poverty is being created day by day. This is an inevitable phenomenon of the current privately owned production society. From this perspective, unless the entire problem is resolved, your family problem will be difficult to resolve. ㈢ Study issues. Since you are doing the hard work of copying from morning until night, it naturally seems that you no longer have the possibility of continuing your studies in terms of economy and time; however, both "specialized skills and knowledge" must be honed and cultivated through the struggle of practical life. If you are good at seizing opportunities and "stealing leisure from busy work" to read and make up for your "skills" and knowledge, it is not without hope of success; with your junior middle school level, you can also learn accounting, bookkeeping, and surveying on your own. As for the cultivation of various common sense knowledge, you only need to take the time to read more books, and you will naturally benefit from opening them. Reading in practical life is more intimate, flavorful, and rewarding than reading in school, which cannot be described in words. For the sake of general public's after-work self-cultivation, this newspaper has set up a circulating library in the Mainland Commercial Center, so that general young clerks and workers have the opportunity to satisfy their intellectual needs. You may also want to borrow some books to read. There are very few good tutorial schools, so if you can work hard to study on your own, it seems that you don't need to try them, which would only waste money and time.

Important Books from the Academia Sinica Stored in Peiping Shipped South 162

Yang Xingfo Goes to Peiping to Negotiate

|Research Work in Peiping Continues as Usual|

(Nanjing, 23rd) The historical and important books stored in Peiping by the Academia Sinica are rare in the world. Recently, the valuable parts will be recorded and shipped south. The Academy approved and issued passports, and submitted 20 boxes for approval. Yang Xingfo went to Peiping on the 12th to negotiate shipping matters. It is reported that the books shipped south include research materials from the Institute of Psychology and the Institute of History and Philology, which will be transferred to Shanghai for storage. Research work in Peiping will continue as usual. Shanghai Education Bureau Organizes Curriculum Compilation Committee 166

Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau previously received the kindergarten and elementary school curriculum standards issued by the Ministry of Education and has issued an order to all schools in the city to implement them from the next semester. However, before the implementation of these standards, considerable preparation should be made for various issues that should be studied, such as the levels and numbers of the new standards. Now, in accordance with the provisions of Article 4 of the Ministry of Education's New Curriculum Implementation Measures, the second and third sections of the Bureau have organized a curriculum compilation committee, and experts from various sections, teachers from affiliated schools, and members of the Bureau have been appointed as committee members. All measures are now being planned and implemented separately.

It was already five o'clock when the meeting adjourned.

Special Report

Preliminary Thoughts on Reorganizing the National Normal School System (Part 1) Luo Tingguang 170

After the failure of the combined middle school and normal school system pilot program (Note 1), all provinces have shown a trend of changing course. Zhejiang took the lead in establishing independent normal schools and rural normal schools. Jiangsu announced the "Outline for Improving Jiangsu Normal Education Plan" in September of the 21st year of the Republic (1932), and from this year, designated Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Taicang, Huaiyin, Donghai, Jiaogao, and other middle schools in the province to specialize in normal education and stop recruiting ordinary middle school students. In the spring of the 21st year of the Republic (1932), Jiangxi also formulated a separate normal education plan for the entire province, ordering the senior high school departments of the original middle schools to stop recruiting normal school students from the next year. The newly established provincial normal school has already been established in Nanchang. Many other provinces are also preparing to reform their systems.

Not only that, Article 5 of the "Educational Goals and Implementation Guidelines of the Republic of China" promulgated by the National Government in the 18th year of the Republic (1929) stipulated that normal education should be "independently established within the scope of possibility." The "Normal School Law" drafted by the Ministry of Education and passed by the Legislative Yuan in its 214th meeting in the 21st year of the Republic (1932) (Note 2) was also promulgated by the Ministry of Education on January 19th of the 22nd year of the Republic (1933), ordering all provinces to handle it in accordance with this law from the next semester of this year. Furthermore, the "Educational Reform Plan" passed by the Third Plenary Session of the Kuomintang Central Committee in December of last year recognized "teacher education" as one of the important educational goals, not only confirming the spirit of independence of normal education, but also making slight provisions for the treatment and service of normal school students, etc. The original proposal was resolved as follows:

"1. Secondary normal education institutions, such as simplified normal schools and normal schools, should be run by the government. 2. Normal schools should be separated from middle schools and established independently. 3. Existing normal universities should strive to reorganize and improve their organization, curriculum, and training to make them suitable for training secondary school teachers, so as to distinguish them from ordinary universities and to seek closer ties with normal schools, etc. 4. Universities should set up teacher training classes. All university graduates who wish to become teachers should enter this class to add one year of education courses to prepare for the selection of secondary school teachers. 5. Normal schools and normal universities do not charge tuition fees. Normal schools should, in principle, provide government-supplied food, lodging, and uniforms. 6. After normal school and normal university students have completed their studies, the Ministry of Education or the provincial education department or the municipal education bureau will assign them to service locations. Graduation certificates will only be issued after the term expires, and they will be free to apply for jobs or further education. Those who evade service or do not serve diligently will have their qualifications revoked and their fees recovered."

It is evident that the independence of normal education has practically ceased to be a problem in principle. However, at the beginning of the reform, there are many complicated matters, and it is difficult to achieve an appropriate solution without comprehensive planning. Based on the spirit of independence of normal education, with reference to the normal school systems of various countries, focusing on the improvement of domestic normal education, I have arrived at the following overall recommendations:

1. Based on the meaning of normal education, use scientific methods to specify the concrete goals of training primary and secondary school teachers. This is the most basic procedure. Based on the national educational goals, specify the purpose of teacher education, and then specify the concrete goals of training teachers at all levels based on the purpose of teacher education. The steps are very natural. The so-called concrete goals refer to the knowledge, abilities, character, spirit, ideals, interests, etc. (Note 3) that teachers should possess, obtained by scientific methods. This is the criterion for implementing teacher education and seeking to connect teacher training institutions at all levels. Unfortunately, this has not been achieved in previous discussions of the normal school system, which is a great pity. 2. All teacher training institutions should adhere to the principle of "impartiality." Normal education is the mother of national education, and its good or bad is closely related to the future of the country. Therefore, various types of education may be undertaken by private individuals, but normal education must be run by the government. This has already become a convention in European and American countries, with no question about it.

Military Academy Leads by One Point in the First Half, Falls Behind in the Second Half

The Whole Game is Infinitely Thrilling, Both Teams Rise and Fall

As a result of last night's fierce battle between the Central Military Academy basketball team and the Xiqing Pirates, they unfortunately lost by four points with a score of forty-one to forty-five, which was taken advantage of by the Pirates. The atmosphere was tense, leading to a white-hot situation. The whole game was infinitely thrilling, rising and falling, and the victory was only decided in the last minute. It can be called the first wonderful performance of this season. In the first half, the Military Academy took the lead by one point, twenty-one to twenty. The Military Academy will rest tonight and fight Mai Ling tomorrow night.

Infinitely Wonderful 172

Last night's dramatic battle was infinitely wonderful, the first of this season. Under the strong defense of a formidable opponent, the Military Academy was able to pounce and score. Li Gongyu's wonderful shots and Wang Shixuan's defense were masterpieces. As for the Qing Pirates, they had never encountered such a strong opponent. The defense was tight and unprecedented. The offense was full of thorns, and there were times when they had the ball but nowhere to shoot. The shooting skills of the two, Qier and Smith, were amazing. Both sides exhausted all their skills.

Unpredictable Situation 173

The changes in the course of the whole game, the thrills within, are difficult to describe in detail. Rising and falling, there was no way to speculate. Sometimes it was a tie, sometimes it was one point up or down. At the beginning of the game, the Military Academy took the lead, the Pirates rose later, and the Military Academy equalized again. The Pirates rose again, and the Military Academy exceeded one point and won. This was the situation in the first half. The Pirates rose up, their momentum was rampant, and they scored continuously, exceeding by four points. The largest distance was as many as ten points. The Military Academy counterattacked and fought to only one point behind, with only two minutes remaining. Unfortunately, the Pirates won four more points. Although the Military Academy made another free throw, the result was a loss by four points.

Lucky and Unlucky 174

The strength of the two teams, the Pirates were only slightly better. The Pirates had a strategy of not disrupting the system. Starting in the second half, breaking through the five-man joint defense of the Military Academy was the reason for their victory. Qier and Smith were confident in their shooting. The danger of Qier was even greater. The failure of the Military Academy can also be called lucky and unlucky. The opportunities to throw the ball were more than the Pirates, but they were all off by inches, or hit the hoop, without falling in, or even entered the basket and came out again. Moreover, Wang Shixuan slipped under the basket twice without scoring, and Li Gongyu missed many shots, only a thread away, which was a pity. The Military Academy's late start was also a mistake.

Scene at the Venue 175

After several advances and retreats, Li Gongyu turned over under the basket, and the ball went in. However, after Smith's free throw and Qier's shot, the Pirates exceeded by one point with a score of three to two. Li Gongyu came again with a ball, and the score was six to three, twice as high as the Pirates. The military momentum was vast, and the whole venue cheered loudly, placing infinite hope on the Military Academy.

Difficult to Separate 176

Chun Qiu

Shanghai Musings 184

— Zhong Xian

New and Old

Shanghai is the entry point for all new things in China. The world's newly invented things, whether they are foreign goods or new ideas, are transported to Shanghai by large ships and then sold and transferred to the interior of China.

Chinese who help foreigners sell foreign goods are called "Jiangwan Ferry." Those who help foreigners instill new ideas have not yet been given a special name. Perhaps in the future they will be called "Foreign Ferry." Because "foreign" is broader than "river," the foreign ferry is greater than the river ferry.

"Shanghai gets the jump on trends" has become a common saying, and Shanghai people are proud of it. This is the result of the foreign ferry's efforts.

Everything is fresh in Shanghai. Shanghai people's every move can be a model for inland people. The "Shanghai style" represents the "new style." In the future, new dictionaries may use the word "Shanghai" to mean "new."

A few years ago, Shanghai people wore tight-mouthed shoes, and villagers going to wedding banquets would hang a white copper "shoehorn" on their waists. Shanghai people smoked cigarettes, and the damp tobacco pipes in the countryside rotted. When Shanghai women wore cheongsams, women from the countryside did not dare to wear skirts when they came to the city.

When Shanghai people die, many use foreign coffins in the style of sleeping boxes. However, Shanghai funerals, except for church members, still use many flag-bearers and umbrella-holders, showing a complete feudal color.

On the asphalt roads of the 20th century, there are parades of thousands of years. The Shanghai people with new minds do not feel that it is out of harmony, but the people in the inland feel very strange!

Shanghai people are new in life, but only after death do they reveal their old fox tails.

Poverty and Life 185

— Miao Shen

The Poorer, the More Artistic

I remember the philosopher Schopenhauer having a novel and witty exposition on poverty. He said: Only poverty can train life; only in poverty can one experience the joys and sorrows of the world. The poorer, the more artistic, because the poorer, the more one can recognize the true face of the world. Finally, Schopenhauer also made this judgment: "Every life should be baptized by poverty."

As for me personally, I have praised the world for the sake of poverty, and I have cursed the world!

I have an uncle who has an unusually optimistic and insightful view of the occasional wealth and poverty in life. He said: Poor people are not all people with weak talents. Many are unappreciated. As for the wealthy, not all of them have become wealthy by relying on their true talents and learning, but mostly by relying on luck. Therefore, whenever someone asks my uncle to borrow money, as long as my uncle thinks it is necessary to lend, he will give it to them no matter how much. My uncle is most opposed to writing IOUs. He said that since he is willing to lend, why write an IOU? Writing an IOU is to look down on the person borrowing money. If he has credit, he will definitely come back to pay it back in the future, otherwise, just consider it a gift to him, because when borrowing, there is always considerable emotion before he is willing to lend it to him. This is because my uncle has also come from poverty, experienced the taste of poverty, and had the training of poverty, so he has a unique view of poverty!

It seems that another sage also had a clear revelation about poverty: He said that if you want to make sincere friends, you must do so in times of poverty and frustration; when you are rich and successful, there are only friends who indulge in wine and meat! It is truly a wise saying. I often see many people in the world who are trapped in poverty, groaning in sorrow and annoyance, which I think is too foolish! God's endowment to the poor is not weak; it gives you sincere friends to warm your life; it gives you ruthlessness and indifference to experience life; for the sake of poverty, it has increased a lot of upward efforts; for the sake of poverty, it has eradicated places of paper and gold intoxication, haha; isn't poverty the most artistic?

Historical Lessons 186

— Jiang Ping

| Starting with the Yangzhou Massacre |

According to historical accounts, during the Yangzhou Massacre at the end of the Ming Dynasty, there were more than 100,000 residents in the city, while the Manchu Qing soldiers who killed anyone they met numbered only 500. Five hundred people slaughtered for ten days without encountering any resistance. This is truly shocking! The shock lies not only in the fierceness of the massacre but also in how easily it was carried out. We think of the painful history of the past, and in sadness, we cannot help but feel a bit of shame.

We all think this way: If the thousands of families in Yangzhou at that time each sent one or two strong men to deal with the 500 Qing soldiers, no matter what the result, it would not have been so tragic.

The "September 18th Incident," the "January 28th Incident," and even the cruelty of Japanese rogues killing Chinese people after the fall of Yuguan are similar to the Manchu Qing soldiers massacring Yangzhou. When they came, they were often in groups of five or six. They ran into a street and killed whoever they wanted. The lives of the residents in the street were in their hands. Although the number of residents was thousands or hundreds of times greater than the Japanese rogues, we only heard of five or six of them acting fiercely there, and we never heard of thousands or hundreds of times greater showing any strength at all. Many lost their lives while trying to escape by chance. Friends, rather than die like this, why not gather together to resist? Resistance will certainly involve sacrifice, but this sacrifice is a sacrifice with a price, at least it can frustrate some of the enemy's ferocity; speaking of the word 'face', it is much more glorious!

Clam 187

— Shi Bing

| Thoughts on the Four Seasons |

It is said that clams are a kind of self-dead worm, then I am just an immature clam.

I don't have any pessimism, I just feel that everything is too empty and lacks vitality.

From spring to winter, the years go by in a cycle. From the motherly spring to the fatherly severe winter, the climate is constantly changing, but I have not realized it at all.

People say that spring has arrived, really, spring has arrived, ah, it only adds to my annoyance; the heavy thunder awakens the life of tree insects, and revives people's youth, but forgets to awaken the deep nightmares of last night. I stepped on the green grass, holding willow branches, chasing the stopped bird sounds; I walked out of the lightly fluttering willow forest again, sending off the setting sun.

The scorching sun arrives, this is summer. The days are even more dull, but so long, I really want to be a Kuafu chasing the sun, chasing this sun, earlier to the west. Ah, hot summer, it is so hot, but it fans the entire earth, but it cannot fan my cold heart.

Seeing that the grass and trees are about to decline again, this is a symbol of my life! Autumn, generally sad.

The harsh winter, the sand-like snowflakes, scattered and flying, it hides the darkness of the world, and builds some light for people. The whole year, only this season gives me some comfort, I often think, stepping on the snow, on this cold winter night, to find some sympathy.

Ah, I am not annoyed, anyway this is not annoyance.

Understanding one's own pain, this is not annoyance. The most annoying thing is that I cannot grasp my own pain. If I can find the answer to what annoys me, I will grasp this point and untie this net that binds my heart. But, ...... expectations are far away.

Novel

Hometown 188

— Hu Tiwei

Second, they only care about driving and don't care about cleaning up the car. Because cleaning up the car is inevitably close to vulgarity and should be handled by a group of short-clothed villagers in C Township. Therefore, a car will not retire until it is on its last breath and terminally ill. Third, in the evening, since there is no official business to handle, they have to gamble to pass the time, and all-night mahjong is very common. Dropping the dominoes and going to drive, although the feeling of the fingertips is particularly sensitive, it is inevitable that there will be a few unlucky travelers who will occasionally receive the gift of stroke cards and become people in deep boudoir dreams. As a result, a group of gentlemen in C Township who know their fate must solemnly and solemnly teach young people traveling to other places:

"You young people only know how to be fast. Humph! C Township's cars must not be tried lightly!" However, Hongye felt that seeing her father's sick face was more important than her own life safety. These newspaper records can only be regarded as exceptions. The stationmaster in his slippers and Zhongshan suit waved the green flag, and seven or eight - perhaps close to twelve or thirteen - short-clothed villagers began to stretch out their hands and push this car, which was full of twenty-six passengers, inch by inch, forward. For a time, the sound of "xie xu" was like being on Shanyin Road.

If it were always like this, traveling on land like a boat, it would be safe. Unfortunately, after pushing about a hundred steps, the front of the car actually rattled and smoked for a while before driving away. Yellow sand rolled behind the car, and white smoke billowed in front of the car. This road was probably built too well, so God secretly circled it. As soon as the car sped up, there was also a kind of stomach-strengthening and spleen-invigorating movement. Hongye's straw hat bumped into the nails on the roof twice, and the accumulated momentum was completely lost.

The car traveled for one hour and forty minutes, and C Township was in sight! Green mountains; precarious city walls; stacked neatly and beautifully, wine jars like small mountains; stone archways built by imperial decree, one by one; these are all characteristics of C Township. Particularly lovely are these wine jar mountains. Each one is round and smooth, arranged like bright pagodas. Hongye had always admired the wine merchants of C Township, who had such amazing skills, and wanted to have the opportunity to see them stack them one by one with his own eyes, but he had never encountered it.

From the bus station to Hongye's home, you still have to take a rickshaw for thirty minutes. In the car, Hongye suddenly felt an inexplicable chill. The closer he got to home, the more flustered he felt. The attack of the storm seemed to be right in front of his eyes. It wasn't until he saw the black-painted wall of the gate in the distance, with the gray wall written with "Tearing Down Posters," and there were no unusual signs, that his heart was only half settled. (III)

Women's Paradise

Miss An 189

— Ms. Hui Zhu

That Miss An makes me feel uncomfortable when I see her, do you know why?

I remember once, I agreed to go out for lunch with her on Thursday. When that day came, she ran to my house after twelve o'clock, opened my drawer, opened my handbag at will, took out a tube of lipstick, and applied it carefully in front of the mirror. My family was already having dinner there, and I went back first because I was going to accompany her out for lunch.

After a while, she applied lipstick and powder, and smiled at me, "Oh, sister, I'm sorry, I'm going to the city to see my mother, but I can't accompany you to lunch. You don't mind, right?" She would say some apologetic words.

This kind of situation has happened many times.

But she herself often likes to suggest going to dinner together, and at the same time, she shouldn't bring others with her, like going to cafes or watching movies, it's all like this.

"Why did you go with Miss Qiong? Leave her quickly. Don't you like the movie starring Hu Die? Let me accompany you." She said possessively.

If you are doing very busy things one night, she will come and talk about some things, saying that she feels that she has been living a very boring life these days, and she has also scheduled ten days in advance, and this Wednesday night, she invited me to her house for dinner.

I was waiting for this day. Mr. Ma asked me to go dancing, and I refused. Miss Lin asked me to go to the movies, and I didn't go. I packed everything up. By then, the clock had chimed seven o'clock. She really came. As soon as she entered the door, she said, "Dinner will have to be rescheduled. Let's reschedule it for tomorrow, because I have another appointment with Miss Pan today."

She also has more things that make people uncomfortable. For example, when the agreed day comes, she comes with others and says, "I'm going with Mrs. He, so you don't have to go. Don't mind." How uncomfortable are these words to hear?

Once, I went to Sincere Department Store to buy something and stopped by to see her. She didn't say anything to me. After I bought my things and went home, she ran to my house to see me, but said that her mother wanted to buy a sanitary shirt, and she didn't have time to accompany her, so she had to have me accompany her. Like this Miss An, she really doesn't understand the principles of social interaction at all. Of course, there are many people like Miss An in this society!

Aesthetics of the House 190

I often go to my friends' homes to observe. Some of them are decorated very exquisitely, and everything can arouse people's interest. Of course, exquisite decorations require a lot of money. Many people have economic difficulties and cannot afford it, but no matter how simple it is, cleaning up is the first priority, because a well-decorated room can arouse people's interest in staying at home. A messy home can often make the husband unable to sit still at home. Here is a picture of the layout of a house, and everything is very simple. This is almost what everyone can afford. Therefore, the beauty of the house does not necessarily have to be very luxurious to be well decorated. Simple and clean also have a kind of aesthetic interest. I think this issue is what the housewives of every family should study.

The Silver and Money Industry at the End of the Lunar Year 196

Unlimited Ticket Collection Time

Influx of Supply Causes Auxiliary Coins to Plummet

The silver and money industry usually extends the ticket collection time gradually during the final closing of the lunar year, starting ten days in advance. The closing time, which is usually 2 pm, is first extended to 3 pm, then to 4 or 5 pm. In the last few days, the deadline is extended without time limit. In recent days, the ticket collection time has been extended, and all procedures have been delayed. It is necessary to work until midnight at the earliest to complete the procedures each day. This year, there is a new phenomenon, different from the previous year, which is the auxiliary coins. In the past, the market prices of various auxiliary coins would soar at the end of the year. This year, however, on days such as yesterday and the day before, they plummeted instead. The reason is that various ports knew that auxiliary coins in Shanghai would soar at the end of the year, so they transported them to Shanghai one after another in advance to facilitate circulation. At that time, they were hoarded by small money houses, so the prices did not loosen. As of yesterday, the influx of supply made it difficult to maintain, and they also sought to sell them one after another. As a result, the prices plummeted from both sides.

A Collection of Overseas Telegrams 204

(Sugar Market) New York, 21st: Spot sugar remains at 6.875 cents, and the market is stable. Futures for January also remain at 7 cents, and subsequent months are mostly one pound higher. March is at 6.9 cents, May at 7.03 cents, July at 7.07 cents, September at 8.01 cents, and December at 8.05 cents. Also, London reports that March is up 25 to 5 shillings. May remains at 5/1.75. August is up 25 to 5/4.25. Java white sugar remains at 7 shillings 9 pence.

The New York sugar market was very weak last week. Total transactions for the week included 186,000 bags of Philippine sugar and 72,000 bags of Puerto Rican sugar. Before the end of the Roosevelt administration, the uncertainty regarding necessary tax rate changes and the recent actions regarding the new Cuban harvest have further increased the supply of Philippine sugar. Although the upward trend in the sugar market has now passed, the hope for better conditions is gradually improving. The supply position of the sugar market in the world seems to be seeing a stable reversal. The decline in refined sugar prices does not lead to increased demand. Best granulated sugar is at 3.90 cents per pound, compared to 3.95 cents last week.

Account Settlement Period Approaching, Rayon Sales Improve 205

As the end of the lunar year approaches, workers in inland silk factories must stop work for the New Year. Yesterday, only the Sichuan merchants, due to the end of the war in Sichuan Province, needed raw materials and replenished seventeen boxes of Grade B Italian-German rayon for January and February at the guild. Prices did not fluctuate much due to the stabilization of exchange rates.
